Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
51
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Path of Heaven
<Prayer> Father, with only about 40 days left in 1971, we hope that You will protect this time.
Looking at the slogan 'Securing a Victorious Unification Foundation', we have gathered our insufficient sincerity over the past 10 months to bring forth an understanding that aligns with Your will.
Father, how much have You labored to lead the children? How much effort have You put into guiding the immature ones? When we think about how much effort You have put into urging these immature beings to their destined place, we must reflect again on how we are always lacking when we face You.
When we think that true sons exist where Your love is present, it should be a joyful place for the true sons who come to You with longing in their hearts. However, when we consider that the heart of the Father, who comes to find children who cannot stand in such places, must always be lonely and sorrowful, we, who know such a Father, hope that the painful path of restoration will pass quickly.
We know well the path of sorrow that You walked to find individuals, families, nations, and the world. As You stood in a careful position, determined for absolute victory with an absolute resolution, how many times did humans on earth fail to decide their positions in front of Your desires, only to rise and fall, becoming exhausted and retreating? Father, we have also come to this place following such a fateful path.
When we see ourselves unable to boast of being in Your embrace today, and when we realize the responsibility we have to protect the remaining path, we understand that fallen humans can never escape the environment of the fallen realm, and that it is difficult to break free from habitual ties. Knowing this, we feel once again that Your position, which drives individuals to break free from such environments, is truly pitiable. We know that even the process of following the driven individuals is a sorrowful path of restoration that You cannot love and embrace.
When we are to be added to the path, it is a path where enemies are stationed to block us, making it impossible to go together unless we clear the way ourselves. When we think of the path of suffering that requires such effort from You, we cannot help but associate the high mountain visible before us with the path You must take. If there is a rugged road, we cannot help but think of the sorrowful heart of the Father on the path of restoration, and we also think that it must be our environment and circumstances as we walk the path of life.
However, when we consider that it is a path we cannot walk according to Your heart, even though You stand in the position of authority governing all people in the realm of victory, we have not truly sympathized with the misery of the Father who comes to gather fallen lives while putting everything behind. Instead of removing Your sorrow from the path You walk, we recall the ancestors of the historical process who inflicted pain and misery upon You.
When we acknowledge that we are descendants of such ancestors, if we feel pity for our own wretched state today, we realize that it is indeed a pitiable state, a miserable state, and a state that no one can sympathize with. When we feel that our Father in heaven has sought out such a group to walk this path, we realize that we have been the ones who have added burdens instead of going.
Father, as time passes and the years go by, we must realize that the truly pitiable one is You, when we think of those who long for the group that worries about not being able to establish the way of filial piety before You. Since the day fallen humanity was met, reflecting on the life of the wandering sufferer, we cannot help but acknowledge that we are a group without face before You. When we think of how much effort You have put into leading the historical process to bring it to the limit of restoration, we must discover once again that we must tighten our belts and resolve ourselves before You.
We must understand that where we desire our hands to rest, Your hands are at work. We must always remember that where we hesitate to take steps, Your tears have left footprints. We know that where our bodies wish to rest, You carry us over rugged valleys and mountains, overcoming countless sufferings, and we must sympathize with the Father who has entered the path of restoration. We must become humans who cannot rest until You rest, yet we must realize that it is we, humanity and ourselves, who make it impossible for You to rest.
Even when we face a comfortable day and smile with vitality, You are the Father who cannot welcome that smile with joy, but rather worries that the manipulation and curse of Satan will remain through that path of laughter. When we think of how serious and how tragic the situation must be for You to urge us, we realize that You are the pitiable one, the lonely one, and the miserable one.
When we think of the one image You seek in the midst of life and death, the Father who longs for sons and daughters, we realize that we are in no position to hope for Your heart because we cannot take into account such a situation. However, when we think that if we are abandoned by You, we will be torn apart before our enemies and disappear as offerings before them, we know that this path is the path of restoration that cannot be given up, the path of life that cannot be forsaken. Therefore, when we consider that countless ancestors have continued this path even while facing death, we realize that following the path You walk is not an easy road.
Yet, even if it is not an easy path, no matter how rugged and long it may be, for humans, that path may end within a lifetime or a century, but for You, there is the responsibility of crossing over the peaks of thousands of years of history. Therefore, when we think about how profound Your responsibility is, even if the cross we bear before ourselves is heavy and large, when we acknowledge that we know Your path and that we have become Your sons and daughters, we must realize that this path is one we cannot avoid.
In such a position, the path of following You is a path of tears, a path of pain, and a path of sighs. We must realize that it is foolish to seek happiness on this earth while tracing the path of faith.
When we look upon Your dignity, we must think that You have the responsibility to bring billions of humanity into Your nation. When we see that our one life has not always run toward You on the shortcut, we must feel how pitiable Your position is, having to block and cross our path to lead us.
Father, at this time, please look upon the children gathered here. We must reflect once again on what we hold in our hearts. We must examine what corner of the path we stand on and what form we are taking, and we must do so from the perspective of the living.
When we consider what position we stand in and what path we are taking, we know that it must be heavenly. Even if we lean on a staff, we must lean on the staff given by heaven, and even if we wear clothes, we must wear the clothes inherited from heaven. When we think that every aspect of our lives must harmonize with heaven, lest we worry about being struck down by the enemy's arrows, we realize that it is indeed a cautious path of life, a path of faith, and a path of restoration. It is a matter of what position we stand in.
Father, may there be a time when we can love You deeply, long for You with all our hearts, and praise Your holiness with our hearts, asking if there has ever been a time in our lives when we could forget everything to do so. If there has not been such a time, we must repent once again for being unfilial children.
When we feel that we are standing at a moment when the hands that should be joined with You cannot be connected even by an inch, we must ask ourselves if there has ever been a time when we were willing to face death to hold onto Your hand, even if it meant falling into the abyss of death. We have not had such times, but when we think of how many times You have faced such moments, we cannot help but acknowledge that we are filled with nothing but shame before You.
Father, come to us at this time. You must occupy our insufficient hearts. We must not be swallowed by Satan, so may You alone govern us and may You alone be present. We must realize once again that we must become a group that sacrifices everything to secure this moment while hoping for tomorrow's victory and overcoming today's rugged mountains.
As the years pass by, as ten years go by, as youth and adulthood pass, and as adulthood turns into old age, when we find ourselves standing in a position where we cannot claim the right to comfort from You or discover the victory of ourselves, we must realize how miserable such a life becomes. We must feel that the coming youth is frightening, and that the coming adulthood is frightening. We must recognize that the old age approaching, looking toward the twilight of life, is a fearful place.
Before that time comes, we must prepare fully, and even if it means dying and dying again, we must pledge victory in the fierce battle, becoming sons and daughters who cannot be erased from Your heart, and becoming heavenly warriors who protect the heights You have occupied. We, these humble bodies, bow before You with the desire to be such.
Father, we must hear the words and counsel that come from Your breath, and we must inherit Your wishes as our own. If You have pledged victory, we must become heavenly warriors who can align with that path of victory. Even if there is a path of judgment that pledges Your final victory and Your ultimate decision, we must choose that path, realizing that it is the way of restoration, as You have said that those who seek to live must die, and those who seek to die will live.
Father, now please gather our insufficient hearts and remember this morning. As we once again meet mid-November, may Your love be with us even more. We earnestly hope and wish to become a group that guards the final path on Your foundation to make the remaining year shine and be glorious.
Please remember the children scattered across the nation, and protect the young daughters who are on the front lines, Father. Please protect the fate of this nation and this people, Father. We must understand that a people unprepared become a pitiable people. We must recognize that unprepared families or individuals become pitiable groups.
Even if there is a source of peace in a place that is complacent, it cannot be something one can possess, and even if there is the authority of victory, one cannot stand on a solid ground of victory. When we think about this, we must feel once again that the children gathered here must fulfill their responsibilities and repay their gifts before You, and that they must become those who willingly walk the path of struggle and suffering to make what remains their own.
May we become a group that entrusts everything to You, discussing and following the path You walk.
When we stand in a position to faithfully understand Your will, we must realize that there is a reason we must bear all burdens and walk the path we do not wish to walk. If we have become those who do not wish for such a path, we must feel that there is no greater shame than this.
Even if my body is crushed and my heart is broken, may we become a group of unity that follows the ties of filial sons and daughters centered around You.
Father, right now, the groups from the universities are gathered in Su-tak-ri, standing at the crossroads of determining this era's mission, receiving training. Please be with them personally. How much arduous adversity have they gone through to reach that place? This country and the university must overcome the final peaks...
When I think about being at a breathless point, the time has come when the young people who must determine the fate of this country tomorrow can be embraced by you, Father, and guided by you. I earnestly ask and hope that you will lead us according to your will, along the path of victory you have desired, so that a day may come soon when the Republic of Korea can raise its hopes and pledge its glory.

Father, the year 1971 is now running toward sunset. When I think about what each of us holds as our wishes, what legacy we leave behind, and what burdens we carry, we must not become a group of light bodies that possess nothing. When looking at the country, I feel the heavy burden we bear, and when looking at the church, I also feel that we are in a position where we must shed the blood of suffering. We are in an urgent and critical time where we must settle all the crosses left for our families and individuals, and dedicate our entire selves for the church and the nation.

Father, you have divided the Republic of Korea with the 38th parallel; please remove the 38th parallel. I know that there are countless emotional stories intertwined with the division of the North and South. There will be many who shed tears while looking toward the northern land, and at this moment, there are also those in the North who are groaning in sorrowful circumstances while looking toward the southern land. I earnestly ask that the fate of this poor Republic of Korea does not end in such misery. I sincerely hope that you will lead us before you so that the time of national repentance may come.

For this to happen, there must first be a group that bears the responsibility of becoming a sacrifice, but we know very well that until now, there has been no such group or religious organization. We understand that established religious denominations are not such groups. When I think about this tremendous fact that it must be us who are insignificant, I realize that the path of the heavy cross we bear must be shared with you, Father. I must have a heart that is willing to take on the burden of that cross, and when I think about not having a place of miserable plight to do so, I realize that those who seek comfort for themselves today can only be a shameful group before you.

Father, the group gathered here has come together to deepen our connection with you and to receive your commands. Please fill our empty hearts with your grace, and let your strong heart come upon our timid hearts so that we, who have wandered in the darkness, may become your reliable children who can joyfully shout for liberation and run vigorously toward the final battlefield. If we cannot do so, we must feel that you will also grieve, and we must pledge to be your children who settle our debts rather than leave behind a legacy of light.

Please look down upon the children scattered throughout the nation at this time, and remember the young children who are struggling abroad in your heart. I earnestly ask that you help us establish a resting place on this dark and harsh land, a quiet place that no one knows. Please take charge of everything. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Those who walk the path of faith are fundamentally different from ordinary people who do not walk the path of faith. Just because they want to go east does not mean we can go east as well, nor can we follow their way of living just because they live centered around themselves.

When we consider the issue of faith, it is easy to think that the paths of believers and non-believers cannot be the same. In the human world, we can easily understand this, and similarly, when we look at individuals in the Unification Church who claim to represent God and all religions, the same applies.

It would be good if the path God wants to take aligns with the path we, the members of the Unification Church, want to take, but as we realize that there is distance between God and us, and that there are barriers that cannot be freely and smoothly connected, we can easily conclude that our believers cannot always match the pace of the path God walks.

If the path we, as members of the Unification Church, are walking is not the same as the path God is walking, what will be the result? When we consider whether the places where God resides and where the members of the Unification Church reside can align, it is inevitable that they cannot.

When we look at the history that our Unification Church has walked so far, it cannot align with the history that God has walked to lead this Unification Church. 

When we reflect on our daily lives centered around individuals, we can feel various transformations in the path we set out on each day. As we consider how long our determination to stand before God will last, we can see that we are not in a position worthy of God's trust to lead us.

When we think about this, if God's path is a high road, then our path must be a low road; if God's path is a straight road, then ours must be a winding road. If God walks in sorrow, we are those who, rather than longing for the path of sorrow, center ourselves on our own happiness and seek our own joyful path. We cannot assume that what we like always aligns with what God likes.

In our daily lives, whether eating or considering the state of the times, we cannot expect that every moment will be a place where heaven is with us, and this is a fact we can understand by looking at our overall living environment.

When we recognize that we are in such a position, we must acknowledge that as the environment changes, the only path left for God to lead us is the path of His labor. In other words, if there is something I desire to be happy about, that desire cannot be something that brings joy to God; it can only become an additional burden to Him. When we think about this, we realize that the longer we are on this path of faith, the more we may leave behind a legacy of sorrow rather than an internal connection that brings us closer to God.

To walk the correct path of faith, if there was a time when God held us and rejoiced, we will always yearn for that joyful time. If such a time existed in the past, we will always compare it to now, lamenting that while it was good then, it is not so now. If we think that the past, which we long for, remains a good memory buried in our internal experiences, that would be a great misunderstanding. If there was a day of joy in the past, how much suffering and sacrifice must God go through to bring that joy back to us today? Knowing that humans cannot awaken on the path of suffering without experiencing something that stimulates joy, we must understand that God must pay a multiplied price of sacrifice to prepare that moment.

Therefore, every time we yearn for a joyful moment, we should reflect on how much shameful suffering we have placed upon God and resolve to never find ourselves in such a position again as we navigate our daily path of faith. If we do not do this, we will not be able to bring forth anything that can alleviate God's continuous sorrow, and the path to draw closer to God cannot remain smooth and joyful; it cannot come as we desire.

Thus, the more we yearn for a good moment, the more we must avoid walking a path that causes God concern. If we can stand in a position to call upon God while punishing and restraining ourselves, that is one thing, but if we seek something that can be better than the past, we will undoubtedly increase God's burden and only hasten sorrow, which indicates that we cannot walk a deeper path of faith.

When we think this way, we must feel that the path God walks and the path we walk always diverge in our lives. Just as you can critically evaluate your daily life centered around yourself, the same applies to your environment. Behind you is your family; behind your family is your nation or the world. Can you lead your family, or your nation or the world, while being centered around yourself? You cannot.

As the connections to your family deepen, you will feel the transformation of your own self, and in relation to God, as the environment expands, it is a fact that the challenges will increase. Therefore, the path of a believer must be simplified. It must be simple. We should not have a complicated environment.

Even if we are in a simple position, we cannot go forward with our own wishes. We cannot say, "I have this plan, and I will go this way." Why? Because the direction of the path he is taking cannot always align with God. Therefore, we must always place God before us and follow Him, and it is not God who must match our pace; we must always be in a position to match our pace to God. Without this, we cannot walk the correct path of faith.

When we think this way, when young people in their youth say, "I must walk this path," can they walk the same path as everyone else in society? They cannot simply walk the same path. They must take a position that is isolated from that environment. The more isolated that position becomes, the closer they will be to the direction God is walking, rather than moving away from it. The easier it is, the further they move away from God. Therefore, the more difficulties one faces on the path of faith, the closer they will be to the path of faith.

The path of faith is the path that follows where heaven goes. 

When we look at the horizon, whether below or above, there is a 90-degree angle; when we look above the horizon, there is also a 90-degree angle. From the opposite perspective, there are 90 degrees, 90 degrees, and 360 degrees that change here. The direction God walks is one aspect, but it is surrounded by 360 degrees. Even on a flat plane, it is like that.

However, God does not walk only from a flat perspective; He walks from a three-dimensional perspective, so the degrees of divergence in the path He must take are multiplied many times over. Therefore, since the path we must take is the path God walks, it cannot be aligned with just that one path.

Just because I suffer does not mean that suffering alone is enough. I must also seek the way. In seeking that way while suffering, I must not be trapped by the bitterness of suffering but must overcome that bitterness through research and regain hope. If I cannot align with the direction God is walking, this is a serious issue.

Is the environment where I live freely and eat according to my own desires a place where God can freely engage with me? It is not. Is the place where I meet my favorite friends a place that God can approach with a good heart? It is also not. Is the family where I live happily, which I consider to be happy, a family that God would recognize as happy? Without a doubt, it is not. Or, is the path I take as a citizen aligned with the direction my country is heading a path that would please God? It is needless to say that it is not.

When our individual paths diverge from heaven, it is only natural that the paths of the environment and the whole will diverge even more from heaven. When we see this, we must conclude that following God is not an easy path. How difficult must it be? We cannot help but conclude that it is an unimaginably difficult path.

Now, when we think about this, are we the only ones? Is it only us who wish to walk the path of faith? No, it is not. When we consider the path God walks, does He walk behind us? No, He must go ahead of us. We are the ones who follow. There is a difference between going ahead and following. The God who goes ahead must fulfill the mission of pioneering, while we do not have to pioneer; we simply need to follow what has been pioneered. If God ascends to a high place, we must follow Him up; if He descends to a low place, we must follow Him down. If God continues toward a flat place, we must follow that flat place endlessly.

In ascending, descending, or following a flat path, the more we criticize with our own minds, even a little, the more it becomes a detrimental path. The path we must take is the path of following; we must match our pace and rhythm to it, and we must do as instructed. 

In the path of faith, if someone cannot stand in a position to say, "I have now arrived at the place I wanted to be on this path of faith; I have achieved everything I desired," then that person cannot have their own claims, regardless of who they are. This is an undeniable fact when you think about it. Therefore, before establishing my own claims, I must seek what God claims. When I reach a position where I can rejoice, that joyful position...
is not a position that can block the path of heaven, but rather a position that can become a sacrifice for the enemy, isn’t it? It is a position that can bring sorrow to God and joy to Satan. When I think about that, I can turn 180 degrees. Just by thinking about it, I must become the kind of person who can transcend that position at once.

Reflect on how wrong your faith path has been. All the senses through which I see, hear, and feel are the same. When looking at daily life, the question is, how will I manage this and align with God? This cannot be a trivial matter. Therefore, it is not a year that is the issue, but a day. Even within a day, it is not the 24 hours that matter, but the emotions I feel at this moment through my senses. The question is whether that is rising vertically toward heaven or whether it is aligned with the upward direction when compared to the horizontal line. This is something that must always be adjusted.

Am I descending below the horizontal line, or am I being pulled down below the line that Satan is dragging me down to? If I find myself in such a position... Even if I cannot stand in the same position as God, am I at least adjusting my relative position and aligning the directions of up and down? When I consider these issues, I must reflect once more on how ambiguous my faith path has been and how much of a position God could trust.

God is leading such a person. In leading, it cannot be a joyful path or a good path. Why? Because there cannot be joy on the path that God walks. It would be a different matter if only humans were being led, but the enemy is waiting outside of humanity.

On the path that God walks, the enemy is always waiting. When I see that enemy, I realize that the enemy is not only personal but also familial, national, and global. It seeks to block the faith path that wants to mobilize this global platform. The global stage is not on heaven's side. It is the tool of Satan, the equipment of Satan, and the weapon of Satan. Satan commands at any time to block the path that heaven wishes to take in every possible way.

Therefore, what kind of path is heaven taking? When heaven must take a step, it cannot avoid fighting against the environment. Without doing so, it cannot proceed. It must remove the obstructing environment and develop a devoted environment; otherwise, it cannot take a step. 

Since God cannot walk alone on that path, He must take humans along. How should He do this? If we focus solely on humans, we cannot advance in a fully coordinated direction. We must move forward while fighting against the enemy behind us.

However, we are not able to follow. The more we cannot follow, the further we drift from God, and the more we become captives of Satan from behind. When there are three or more captives, no matter how powerful God is, He must retreat and set conditions of lamentation before Him, leaving no record of victory. When it comes to that, how much debt do we owe to God in our faith journey today, and how shameful have we become? This is an undeniable fact when we look back at our faith life and life journey.

Satan has blocked the path that God walks for 6,000 long years. He knows well what has been blocked. So when can God walk on a flat path? That time must go through an era that has never existed in the historical age until now. When will it be that God can rest? That time will begin when the humans living on this earth have truly received the second liberation and stand at the forefront, placing God behind them and taking on the full responsibility to fight against Satan on behalf of God. That is when it begins. If not, hoping that God will rest before Him is an illusion. This is how it is.

Blessed are those who endure to the end. Today, we who are living a life of faith are faced with this urgent global situation. Until now, God has paid the price of countless sacrifices to create a democratic world and a Christian cultural sphere. But where is this democratic world and Christian cultural sphere heading? When we look at Christianity, it seems to be going its own way. If there is a specific denomination, that denomination follows the will of its founder.

There are many sects. While there are many sects, the true path that a sect should take, the path that goes with God, is not two paths but one path. What kind of path will that one path be? If we are to find it, there must be an easily discoverable path. What is it? In this age, if there are those who are willing to endure hardship and suffering for the proposition of heaven, even if they are not united, they are still not a group that is stumbling in the direction they should go among religions. If there is a group that God can think of as having a connection on earth, it cannot be anything other than such a place.

That is why the Bible says that those who endure to the end are blessed. Enduring to the end is not an easy task. The end does not simply mean that I can die alone. There is an end for a family that can be entirely sacrificed. There is also an end for a nation or a world.

Thus, the term "to the end" does not refer to a position where one can fight based on a familial standard; it refers to a position that transcends that, not merely the end of a national struggle but the end viewed from the highest point, and not just the end of the world but the end that can be declared after passing through the world.

When considering these issues, how great will the suffering be until we follow the path of faith with God, transcending individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world? When we think that there must be someone who must walk that path throughout their life or lifetime, those who seek that path cannot hope for peace, rest, hope, or glory to reach the end.

That is why the Bible says, "Those who seek to lose their life will find it." It is not about living in a position where one puts oneself forward to seek something. It is those who seek to die who truly live. Only those who seek to die can determine victory as individuals. Those who do not wish to die with their families cannot meet the end they should reach with God. This is beyond question. The same applies to nations; if one does not wish to die with their nation, they cannot meet the end that the nation should reach with God. The same goes for the world.

When we think about such conclusions, when have you stood at the end? Have you ever tried to find a position that can be the end for individuals, families, tribes, nations, or the world? How much has God longed for that end to come? I believe that God hopes for the end of my individual life to be at this moment. He hopes for it to be at this moment, but when you consider how much you have vowed to determine your individual end at this moment, if you discover that you have not done so, you must once again completely overhaul your faith attitude. You must kill yourself. Your current faith posture is fundamentally and essentially unacceptable, and you must ruthlessly break it down and start anew.

So when can a family stand at the end? When can a nation say it has come to the end? When can the world say it has reached such a position? Is that not the position that God wants to establish? Therefore, if you think that the saying "Those who seek to die will live" can be easily taught in a comfortable and natural environment, that is a great misunderstanding. The saying "Those who seek to die will live" is a testimony of heaven. It is a testimony of God Himself. You must understand that it proclaims the inner workings of God's life.

We must realize anew the fact that heaven is weaving a path of struggle prepared for death. It is impossible to desire to die. This statement itself is contradictory. However, because this fallen world is a world of contradictions and oppositions, the only way to rise from the place of death to the place of life is to completely deny oneself at the ultimate extreme, which is nothing but death.

From that place of death, the ties with the world are severed, and a new connection with God is established. At that moment, one is separated from one and reunited with another, so the standard of the offering that heaven desires can only be found in that place. We must think that God could not help but give such a command.

The path that God walks and the path that we humans walk cannot be different. Of course, humans and Satan are different. That is why you must know that heaven and Satan are in direct opposition.

Knowing that God must fight against the enemy from behind, you should be able to say, "Heaven, do not forsake me. I will lead the fight. Even if you do not look after me directly, I will boldly walk the path you take. Let us hurry and walk this path." Only then can God defend against the enemies that confront me and fight on my behalf. Moreover, by aligning my actions with that, I can escape from the world of enemies and break through Satan's encirclement. Otherwise, heaven cannot take me along.

When viewed in this light, how dangerous it is to say, "Heaven, help me!"? Even if one enters a position where their life may end, if one says, "Heaven, do not take care of me, but hurry and go to the more serious place you must go," is that not a position of taking responsibility for leading this group before God advances toward the enemy?

There is an enemy before the path that God must take. If the direction is slightly off here, one can be attacked at any time. Therefore, the desire for heaven to protect me and not look after me while advancing is the path that a believer must take and the essence of faith life.

Look at today’s Christians or pastors; when they pray, they all ask God for something. Centered around their children, they say, "Please do this," or centered around their church, they say, "Please do this." How has a denomination that has prayed like this for thousands of years become powerless? It is because they have fallen into an environment separate from the direction that God plans and the battlefield where God is fighting.

No matter how much they cry out to God, they are placed at a distance where God cannot reach or come. When mobilizing the family, if it is good for oneself, go; if it is not good, do not go—try doing that. Do you think someone is doing it because they like it? You and I are enemies, right? It cannot be like that, and it cannot be done because there is no other way, so it is commanded.

If you want to go up on the path of restoration, you must go down deeply. 

Everyone, when you climb a high mountain in Gangwon-do, the higher you go, the more rugged it becomes. Why is it rugged? If it were flat, people could walk, but the higher you go, you don't see a single dog or a single bird. The higher you go, the more rugged it is. So, as you go higher, you think, "Oh my! My worries are as big as a mountain." Therefore, when climbing a mountain, if you look up at the peak and think, "How can I get up there?" you won't make it. You must look at your feet. Only then can you go. You cannot say, "I will go to heaven." You cannot go by thinking about going up. Think about going up, and you will find that you cannot go. You must look at your feet and take one step at a time. Then you will go.

That is why there is a secret for those who go up and down mountains. They do not look at the peak. If they look at the peak, they will tire out and fall. "How high is this? No matter how high it is, even if it is one step higher, it is not much." They must think like that. But if they look at the peak, they think, "Oh my, it's so high..." So they walk while looking at their feet. "I can see it below my eyes..." they say. If they look up, they will fall.

In the same way, when you walk the path of will, you should not have the mindset of trying to enter heaven. So what mindset should you have? "I am doing this for my neighbor. I am doing this to make those people better." That is the path to heaven. "I am doing this to save those people." That is going to heaven. If you do that, it may seem like you are going down, but you are not going down. You are going up. It is the opposite. The more you go down, the more you go up. Where is there such a good law?

If you go up, you may not know, but the more you go down, the more you go up. If there is such a path, would you go down or not? Everyone, try climbing a mountain once. When you reach the top of the mountain, it feels really good. The air on the other side of the ridge and the air on this side is just a step apart, so what difference does it make? However, the feeling of being at the top is different from the feeling before climbing. When you stand at the top and take a breath, it feels like the air of a different world.

But if there is a way to go up while going down, would you go down or not? Even if you are told not to go down, you will go down. If there is a way to go up while going down, where is there such a good thing? If there is such a path, who would not want to take it? No one would say they won't go.

In the path of restoration, if you want to go up, you must go down deeply. Isn't that a good thing? It is just like a rubber band. Let's think about it. If you tie a rubber band to a large branch of a tree and pull it, it stretches and goes down. It is not easy to go down. After going all the way down, if you just release the tension, it will spring up. When you go up, will you go lower than where the rubber band was tied or higher? You will go higher. You will automatically go higher than the position where it was tied. The history of restoration is that level.

That is why it is said to sacrifice. Sacrifice is good. I am working hard to make all the members of the Unification Church suffer to the point of death. Does that feel bad or good? If you want to sacrifice, you must go down. You must go down to the point of breaking. But what do you hold onto while going down? You must hold onto the will. It is like a rubber band. The more you go down, the higher you can go. I did not perish because I knew that. That is the principle.

When we look at these various issues, preparing a unification plan is not easy. Even when looking at you as individuals, how hard is it for individuals to become one? How hard is it for families to become one? I cannot do it by myself, but it is possible when I hold God's love and God's will. Do you understand? "Yes." What about God's love? After knowing God's love, the unification plan comes out automatically. What about God's will? After knowing God's will, the unification plan comes out automatically. Is that good or bad? "Good." If presenting that plan is the Unification Church, then the Unification Church is good, good, good.

When we look at the slogan "Securing the Foundation for Unification" that we have raised, to secure the foundation means to become a horizontal line. Do you understand? As individuals, you must draw a horizontal line centered on the vertical line and gradually expand it to the family and the church. If you do not match the auxiliary and there is a hole in the horizontal line, do not regard that which has fallen. There is no need to look back at that.

You must understand this and, with only two months left in 1971, centered on this year's slogan of "Securing the Foundation for Unification," you must at least establish a point of emotional unity and move forward. I hope you have this mindset as you meet today, the first day of November. Do you understand? "Yes." Let's sing "The Song of Unification" once. (Singing "The Song of Unification" and concluding the meeting) *

Children's Day and Its Mission

<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is October 1, 1971, in the lunar calendar, and November 18 in the solar calendar. It has been exactly 11 years since this day was set in 1960 to proclaim a new day on this earth, and we are celebrating the 12th Children's Day.

On this day, in the presence of heaven and earth, and all creation, we hold a ceremony before You, and we hope that Your glory may come upon this headquarters as the little children gather here once again at this time. With the same grace and love, Father, please come to us and be with us eternally with Your infinite mercy, love, and compassion.

We are well aware that many spirits who have gone to the spirit world have devoted their lives to upholding Your will throughout the historical course until now, and they hope to restore and resolve through the earth. We also know that those on this earth are putting forth all their efforts to mobilize their descendants to seek a path toward one world. In light of this, we understand that the Unification Church on this earth has a significant mission to represent the mission of the nation and the world, and that we must establish the relative standards You require to achieve both internal and external unity on a cosmic level.

Carrying such a mission, we have come this far through dozens of life courses. Father, we know how much You have labored until now, and how many difficult turning points we have faced, but because You have protected us with Your grace and love, we have remained until this hour, and we thank You for that grace.

This day represents the year 1971. Among the four major holidays we celebrate, this day is the last holiday of the year, so please bless this understanding. Parents' Day, Children's Day, All Things Day, and God's Day—this tremendous historical origin that we have decided with our insufficient devotion has not only been determined in the human world but also in the spirit world. When we see that many people in the spirit world pursue and testify to this day, we feel even more deeply that the mission of the Unification group gathered here is indeed great.

We know how much You have labored to reach this day. Moreover, to fulfill the mission of the children, we must pass through the path of the servant of servants, the servant's path, the path of the adopted son, and the path of the son to rise to the position of the parents. When we think about the sacrifices our ancestors have made throughout history to come to this point, and when we consider that we must overcome the path of suffering to resolve the grief of Eden for not being able to uphold the dignity of the children, we cannot be indifferent today.

As we feel the historical mission weighing down on our shoulders, we also see the global realities and social trends approaching us, and we feel that we are in urgent times. In such times, we must realize that Your trust in us is strong, and that Your earnest heart, which longs for us to fulfill the heavenly mission, is connected behind us in a way that no one can fathom.

Father, please bless this day. Please remember the Unification group. In front of this nation and this world, we solemnly build an altar and, with a heart of connection before You, we know that we have a solemn and historical mission to offer as a substantial sacrifice to restore all things, so please be with us. From beginning to end, please be with us.

As we have kept the path we have walked until now, until we sing the song of victory, please join us. Do not cast us into the world of Satan, and even if You push us into the path of suffering, Father, we earnestly ask and hope that we may be the remnant who can praise the day of victory with You in the place of glory.

On this day, may infinite love be with the group that is pouring their hearts into this place, and may You grant them uniform grace so that they can hold onto the bond of life and praise. Father, we earnestly wish and hope for this. Moreover, we have received news that children scattered throughout the world are putting forth much effort to commemorate this day. Please be with them as well.

Father, if there are those who remember this day in lonely places and shed tears in their hearts, please grant them Your infinite love and many times the grace to remove their lonely positions, and protect them with a strong and grateful grace. 

As we gather our insufficient devotion at this time on this day, we ask that everything we pursue before You may not go against Your glory and hope."
I earnestly ask that the path of the grace of Manmanse be with us on our journey. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> As you all know, today is Children's Day. There are countless countries and many religious organizations on this earth, but there is no day like Children's Day, Parents' Day, All Things Day, or God's Day that we observe in the Unification Church. We have four major holidays: God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day, and today, centered on the year 1971, is the last holiday of Children's Day.

God, who has carried out the providence of restoration centered on religion, As you know, due to the fall of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, God's purpose of creation, in other words, God's ideal of creation, was not fulfilled. Because humanity fell, the purpose for which humans were created could not be realized.

God could not leave that unfulfilled purpose as it was, so throughout human history, He has sought to reclaim it alongside fallen humanity. In order not to stand in the place of failure, God has been engaged in a historical struggle to fulfill His purpose once again.

In this struggle, with whom has He fought? He has fought alongside those who believe in God, alongside those who wish to follow God's path. So, who are the groups that have taken on that mission in the historical process? They are the people of faith. Among religions, there are various faiths, but there will be central religions among them.

When we look at an individual, the one who thinks of themselves the most is their parents. There is an unbreakable blood relationship between parents and children, and all emotional factors of the parents are reflected in the children. Because children are inevitably the result of their parents, parents who have that emotional connection cannot help but think of their children. Regardless of whether anyone else thinks of them, parents always think of their children day and night, throughout all seasons, and we feel this well within our personal lives.

According to where God's emotional connection can be established, God also advances the history of restoration following the places where emotional connections are made with humans. It is the history of salvation. When we consider which religion has more emotional content, which is more earnest, and how much emotional inner responsibility is taken before God in the historical age, the loving God cannot help but align Himself with the religion that has a closer emotional connection.

From this perspective, what religion is that? It is Christianity. Looking at the doctrines of Christianity, the essence of what Jesus claimed is love. The ultimate conclusion He reached is the concept of the bride and bridegroom. This concept has been established.

The central religion of the providence of restoration is Christianity. Jesus emphasized that He is the only begotten Son before God. If God is to love, He does not love just anyone; even if there are other sons, He loves the only begotten Son first. Because there is only one son, He stands in a position to monopolize all that love. When we consider Jesus' declaration of pride in being the only begotten Son, what is that pride? It is that He can receive love from God before anyone else, as a representative who can receive total love. From that standpoint, He possesses unique content.

Furthermore, regarding humans, He said to His followers, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." Here, the bride and bridegroom refer not to the relative relationship of human brides and grooms but to the bride and bridegroom centered on God's love. Jesus Christ is the one who stands as a love-centered being whom God can love as a man, as a son, and as a central being of love in the relative world on this earth. That is why He referred to His followers as brides. Considering the emotional issue of the bride and bridegroom, this is the highest path centered on God's love and can only be the one and only path.

Moreover, Jesus spoke of the bond of brotherhood. He did not call them servants but referred to them as friends or brothers. The terms friends and brothers do not refer to friends born through worldly connections or brothers born through blood relations in the world, but rather to a brotherly bond centered on God's love.

In light of these facts, Jesus referred to Himself as the first son centered on God and demanded the standard of the bride as the relative object of that son. Furthermore, He introduced the inner bond of brotherhood and friendship. This was not merely an introduction of such content centered on Jesus Christ Himself but rather centered on God. Considering this fact, it is undeniable that He presented a core of love that no other religion possesses.

From that perspective, throughout history, while there have been countless religions, if there is a religion that can be considered central in God's historical providence, it can only be concluded that it is Christianity as introduced by Jesus Christ.

From this viewpoint, Christianity, which receives God's love, must develop. Since Christianity is receiving God's love, Satan, who does not like that, must vehemently oppose it. 

If there are those who are filial to their parents and those who are unfilial, the filial ones become the targets of condemnation by the unfilial ones. When a filial child diligently honors their parents, the conditions of that filial piety become the materials and requirements to condemn the unfilial, so the more unfilial one is, the more they will regard the filial person as an enemy.

In the same way, if there are those who receive God's love and those who are filial before God, Satan, who becomes God's enemy, cannot help but condemn that person more than anyone else. Living in a world of evil, Satan cannot allow those who say they will be filial before God to exist, so he drives them into the worst pit and pushes them into the most severe path of death.

In this light, the religion that has overcome the miserable fate of history is Christianity. Christianity has historically developed through the blood of the martyrs. Because Satan hates and despises those who are filial to God more than anyone else, it is an undeniable fact that Christianity has faced harsher trials and persecutions than any other religion.

Thus, Christianity has developed on the foundation of the martyrs who have sacrificed their lives throughout history. Therefore, in the overall providence of history, the central religion that God can provide must be Christianity.

What is the purpose of Christianity sacrificing so much throughout history? The purpose is not to sacrifice individuals in that era. The goal is to pay the price of sacrifice to ultimately subdue the world of Satan and completely suppress and subdue those who oppose and become enemies of heaven, looking forward to the time when they can testify through their mouths, "You have served God with loyalty and filial piety throughout the historical age." This is how it is viewed.

The filial children that God testifies to cannot remain as filial children at the end of this world or the end of the historical age. For example, many parents would call their sons filial if they are filial to them. Their relatives would also affirm them as filial. This is because historically, the way of filial piety is such that the people in that environment can affirm it as valid. However, what is a true filial child? When those who are enemies say, "If I were to choose a true filial child, it would be so-and-so, the son of my enemy," then that person would finally become the greatest filial child in the world.

From this perspective, among those who believe in religion today, who can be a true filial child who can receive God's love, or a loyal subject who has devoted themselves before God? God cannot decide that. Even if God has made a decision, that person cannot be a complete filial child or loyal subject. Even if God praises them as His son...

As you know about Job, when he was blessed by God and served God in a good position, Satan accused him. Because God had given him blessings, anyone could accuse him of being able to like God. However, when entrusted to Satan, God said, "Test whether this person is filial before heaven." Then Satan said, "Yes, I understand. I will do it." He subjected him to all kinds of humiliation and adversity, pushing him here and there, pulling him up and down, and no matter how much he was driven to the brink of death, when he continued to show unwavering sincerity, Satan would say, "I cannot touch him. Even if a year, two years, or ten years pass, his sincerity remains, and I can no longer touch this person." When that happens, he would come before God and say, "God, just as You said, this person is undoubtedly a filial child." At that moment, that person would become a global filial child.

From this perspective, what did Jesus hold onto when He went toward the final path of the cross? Jesus was determined to walk a path that even Satan could not deny, and because He had the capacity to bless even His enemies, God positioned Jesus among His enemies and testified that He was the Son of God. I believe there is also an inner story behind this. In this light, Christians who believe in Christianity must inherit the duty of true filial piety before God.

Jesus Christ came as God's only begotten Son to fulfill the duty of a filial child before God and to fulfill the duty of a loyal subject as a representative to establish the Kingdom of Heaven, ultimately sacrificing His life. Therefore, Christians who inherit His thoughts should not narrow their scope but rather expand it. Furthermore, they should testify not only centered on the nation of Israel but globally.

For this reason, Christianity has expanded the scope to testify that "Jesus Christ is the Son of God who receives God's love, the filial child of heaven, and the loyal subject of heaven," while paying the price of countless sacrifices. When this struggle can be expanded, Christianity has always developed. When such struggles arise, God cooperates, but we must understand the historical fact that when claiming ecclesiastical authority in a comfortable position, God has never cooperated.

Then, in a true sense, where is the filial child that God desires today, the loyal subject that God desires? Has there been such a person in the course of human history? This is the question. Jesus, when He came to this earth, may have fulfilled filial duty as the only begotten Son, but He did not fulfill the responsibility of a loyal subject in establishing the Kingdom of Heaven. When standing on the stage of the struggle to establish a nation, Jesus did not say a word or take any action. Furthermore, did He stand on the stage to present the world before God, saying, "This is how the world should be before God," and instructing all people, "You should follow the path I take"? Did He stand on the stage to confront Satan and testify that Satan is God's loyal subject for the world? He did not.

He did not stand on the stage of the nation, nor did He stand on the stage of the world. As an individual, He stood in the position of a filial child before God as the only begotten Son, but did He stand in the position of a loyal subject representing the nation and the world? He did not.

The issue is becoming a child whom God can love. When we think about this, what do the members of the Unification Church desire today? They desire to become sons and daughters whom God can love. This is the first issue.

Next, what is it? It is to be someone whom God can truly love... You see, there are many kinds of love. In the realm of fallen rights, there are Satan, God, and then people. When we observe the people of the world, the love that people claim to have centered on families is love among people. People can also love in partnership with Satan or love in partnership with God. We can see three types of love here. God does not desire love among people. He does not want love in partnership with Satan. He only wishes for a way to love alongside God.

However, the people of this world live without even considering these standards of love. Even among those who believe in religion, there are few who think this deeply. They say, "Isn't it enough to believe in Jesus and go to heaven?" This is a serious problem.

If God is our Father and we are God's sons and daughters, can those who cannot have a loving relationship with their parents grow up? Such people are orphans. Even if they grow up, they are orphans. For a specific decision to be made that they are not orphans, there must be a mother and father who gave birth to them. When they grow up in the realm of love where their parents love them day and night, they are happy children who have parents. Those parents never withdraw their love for their children, day or night. Because they are within the realm of their parents' love, they are happier than orphans.

Furthermore, what is the reason for a happy wife or a happy husband centered on their spouse? It is because the realm of love centered on the couple involves their entire daily life and activities, and when that realm of love is not withdrawn and remains with them, that couple is said to be happy. Isn't that so?

The same goes for brothers who love each other. Wherever the elder brother goes, the younger brother must go with him. The bond of love must be established together. If there is an elder brother who loves his younger brother, then wherever the younger brother goes, the elder brother can always go with him, and wherever he goes, they can stay together, and that is what we call loving brothers. Isn't that so?

If there is a patriot who loves their country, what kind of person is that patriot? It is someone whose loving heart is always with the nation. Regardless of whether they are miserable or prosperous, or whether they have caused an accident, anyone who lives with a heart that loves all the citizens of their country is called a patriot. This is an undeniable fact.

Because the ancestors of humanity fell, God could not stand in a position to love us humans. If He loved, it would lead to trouble. He would be slandered.
is the fall of humanity. For God to love humanity, there must be content that aligns with that love. This is what has led to the fall.

No matter how much humans establish families, God cannot love those families. No matter how much humans create nations, God cannot love the sovereignty of those nations. No matter how much the world is formed, God's love cannot coexist with that world. It is said that God cannot be with that sovereignty.

What happens when one enters into God's love? 

Then what kind of love is present there? It is the love of Satan. The love of Satan is present. The environment in which each of you lives is surrounded by the realm where Satan can love. This is how it is. The realm of Satan's love...

What is Satan? He is the enemy of God. When God tries to go to the right, Satan tries to go to the left. They are in opposing positions. When God says to do good, Satan says to do evil. He encourages love for the bad.

These days, young men and women are wandering around cabarets or dance halls. Even teenagers are doing so. But while doing this, do they feel joy in their true hearts? Their true hearts dislike it, but they are forced to go along. Behind this, there are threats, coercion, and intimidation. If they don't go, their lives are at stake. You can see that such social environments are prevalent around us. In such places, God's love does not dwell. When the evil and bad results become generalized and the national ideology is eroded, that nation will perish.

Evil will perish. Therefore, all such things must be prevented. Then, a greater path must be presented, but there is no path to present. So it becomes a big problem. It is in conflict with conscience.

However, when one enters into God's love, what happens? There is harmony with conscience. When you experience grace, it feels like you are welcoming a spring day. If you were to describe what a spring day is like, you would say it is good in various ways, but there is nothing to boast about. In some ways, a spring day feels more like a foggy day than a summer day or an autumn day. And when you see the haze rising, it feels like heaven and earth are touching, which can be suffocating. Isn't that so? Rather, a spring day lacks the refreshing taste of winter and only brings a feeling of suffocation. When you can't see the mountains clearly and are surrounded by an environment that feels enclosed, you might wonder what is so good about spring...

But spring is good. Why is it good? Because new life sprouts. All new movements begin from there, starting to operate towards a three-dimensional world. It is a time when one reveals their own value in their own way and shows their inherent beauty, marking the beginning of infinite development, which is why spring is good.

In spring, flowers bloom. Flowers must accompany fragrance. In the terminology of our Unification Church, it is a time when three-dimensional interactions occur that cannot be found in other seasons. Moreover, it is a time when it is not one-sided but can flow in all directions. Because you can feel emotions in all directions, your body feels uplifted. You feel a kind of high-voltage sensation in a higher realm without knowing what your body is. Thus, spring is indeed good.

Similarly, when you go to a place of grace, you will feel your heart rising infinitely. Why is that? What the true heart requires is not to remain within the realm of human love based on human love. If God is a Father, humanity wishes to live immersed in the love of that Father. The original purpose of God in creating humanity was to allow them to feel and live within that realm of love. Because we have the nature given by God to live in such a way, our conscience demands it. Therefore, when that nature touches your heart, you inevitably feel explosive shock and emotion. That is why the place of grace is a precious place that cannot be exchanged for anything.

So what kind of place should the Unification Church go to? It must go beyond the place where God's will has not been fulfilled. Because it has not stood in the place of fulfillment, it must step over that place. To step over, one must become a son or daughter of God. To become a son or daughter of God, one must enter into a realm where God cannot help but think of them day and night.

Humans born into an environment opposing freedom and happiness

Originally, humans should have been born into an environment where they are free in all directions. They should have been born as such, but because they were born as fallen descendants, they suffer from an environment that is the complete opposite.

Sometimes, when you see babies who come out crying and frowning, you realize they are fallen descendants. If humans had not fallen and were born without frowning but instead laughing, how wonderful would that be? When a mother sees a baby crying right after birth, it is serious. The baby flails its arms and legs upwards. This happens every day. Ladies, pay attention. You can feel the baby kicking and flailing in the air. When you hear the crying, it feels like the baby is rebelling against God because it was born as a fallen descendant. It does not feel like it is beckoning heaven to come. Even if it cries, shouldn't the way it cries be a bit different? Ladies, pray. When a baby is born and cries, think of it not as an unpleasant cry but as a pleasant one... Isn't that right?

If you quietly observe people crying in the world, when you ask them, "Why are you crying?" they all say they are crying for themselves. Have you ever heard someone say, "I am crying because of my wife, because of my husband, because of my brother..."? When you see them crying, if you look closely at the root of it, they say, "I am crying because I am feeling sorry for myself."

So, why did the history of tears begin with self-pity? When you reflect on the history of tears, how did it come about? "I am crying because of my mother and father. Isn't that right, mother and father?" If that were the case, it would not be bad. "I am crying because of my siblings. Siblings, isn't that right?" If they agree, then those tears are good, not bad. What do you think?

If the world were filled with such tears, would you want to live in that world or not? Have you thought about it? If such a world existed, you would want to live right in the middle of it. "Why don't you accept my love when I love my mother and father?" you would cry. "Why don't you recognize my love for my siblings?" Even though that unrecognized love ultimately returns to oneself, there is no such type of crying in this world. Everyone is crying for themselves.

I do not believe that God is dead. Do you cry when you are happy? "Yes." When you are sad, do you cry openly? When you are sad, you cry loudly, but when laughter bursts forth, do tears flow? When laughter becomes excessive, tears come out. Isn't that so? When those tears come, you laugh and say, "Oh, I wish these tears wouldn't come, but why do they keep coming?" You dislike the tears but laugh while crying. So, is crying while laughing good tears or bad tears? They are good tears. They are good tears, yet people dislike the tears that come out while laughing and think that the tears shed from sadness are natural. This is strange. There are many such conflicting issues. However, this time is not a time to discuss such things.

So, who is the ancestor that created the history of tears? Who is that ancestor? You all cry, right? Have you seen your mother and father cry? You probably have. You may not have seen your grandparents or great-grandparents cry, but did they cry or not? Anyone who says they didn't is a bit mentally challenged. They all cried, right?

Then, if you trace back to the very last ancestor, there must be a history of tears. Who is the ancestor of the history of tears? The first person is Adam and Eve. Where did Adam and Eve's tears begin? It is because one reaps what they sow; they must shed tears according to what they have sown, so humanity must cry in the same way.

The motivation for humans to cry

So how did Adam and Eve begin to cry? This is the question. Did Adam and Eve cry tears of joy saying, "Oh, Father, how wonderful!"? Did they shed even a few drops of such tears? Did they stop crying altogether, or did they shed at least one drop of tears? What do you think? Our ladies tend to cry easily, whether it is a little bump or a big bump, right? The champions of crying are usually women rather than men.

Do you think Adam and Eve cried tears of joy? Have you thought about it? If they had cried tears of joy every time they met God, they would have absolutely followed God around. "Oh, Father, I can't go. I won't let you go. Where are you going?" They would have said that. If that were the case, would Satan have had time to follow them around? Would the archangel have had time to come and do this and that? There would be no time for that. Isn't that so? But they wandered around aimlessly and ended up crying.

When they were cast out of the Garden of Eden, they must have cried. Did they cry when they were cast out or not? Let’s take an example of a well-off lady. If she thinks, "My husband truly loves me, and my children love me, so I am happy," but then she is forced to be cast out by her husband, would she be happy? She would be unhappy. However, if there is a place where she can shed joyful tears despite being sad about being cast out, then she is not unhappy. A woman who can have a place to rejoice and shed joyful tears, even if she is cast out, is not a miserable person.

In this regard, when you cry, you should not cry for yourself. The reason Adam and Eve cried was that they were trying to assert themselves, fill their own bellies, and elevate themselves. Ladies, do not forget this. Adam and Eve came out waving their flags centered on themselves and dancing, and that is how they ended up. That is why in the religious world, it is said, "Do not be proud. If you come out centered on yourself, it will be a big problem." It is simple. If you come out centered on yourself, you will surely end up like your ancestors. You will be surrounded by sad tears and perish.

When you see the situation where crying occurs, it begins with personal crying, and then it leads to crying at funerals. There, collectively, they cry out, "Oh, oh!" Even though some might be crying insincerely, putting that aside, there is a collective crying. When one's mother or father dies, or when a loved one dies, they do not think about dignity or reputation and cry out, stomping their feet. After that, there is no more crying.

But those who believe in religion are a different kind of group. They are a strange group. They just cry when they bow down. They do cry, but it is different. For example, Unification Church members cry easily. Of course, they cry when they repent, right? When they repent and cry, God watches quietly and says, "Ah, I see you are like that." When they shed tears of repentance, God opens His eyes that were closed and smiles, saying, "Oh, really?" This is the time for repentance.

After such repentance, if one says, "God, now that I have repented, I must be elevated," God will say, "Ah, you will become another second Adam and Eve." He will close His eyes again. It is inevitable. If that happens, it is no different from Adam and Eve. Do you understand? That is how it becomes.

Eve also tried to elevate herself, and Adam also tried to elevate himself, making God feel regret, and they cried and perished. So now, they say, "I do not want that anymore. I will return to the original world. I will walk the path of God's will," and they shed tears of repentance, and God opens His eyes. But if they then say, "I have found the way to receive blessings, so God must also be a God who is for me," then God will retreat. That position is exactly the same as that of the fallen Adam and Eve.

Therefore, after repentance, what should one do? "Even if I die, even if I perish, even if I receive the worst insults in the world, even if I am beaten and torn apart, let Your will be fulfilled through me. Do not fulfill it personally, but fulfill it globally." Then God will say, "Ah, this person is useful." I have realized this. (Laughter) "I am a person destined to die, so You cannot treat me as such, but if there is something You need to toil and suffer for, whether You beat me, eat me, or make me eagle food, I will become fertilizer and compost for Your labor for the world." Then God's eyes will open wide.

Whose benefit is that for? It is not for the person who repents and prays. Who is it for? It is for God. Therefore, it is different from the fallen ancestors Adam and Eve. Because it is different, God intends to leave such a person as a seed for humanity.

What kind of person was Jesus? Now, going back, what kind of person was Jesus? Did Jesus shed tears or not? In the Bible, it is written that Jesus lamented, "Capernaum, will you be exalted to heaven? You will be brought down to Hades." (Luke 10:15) and also lamented, "Jerusalem, Jerusalem, you who kill the prophets and stone those sent to you, how often I have longed to gather your children together, as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings." (Matthew 23:37) He wept while lamenting. 

Furthermore, there is a record that Jesus wept when He raised Lazarus from the dead. In the Bible, there are only two places where it is recorded that Jesus wept.
When Jesus went the way of the cross, He must have cried. So, was that cry for Himself or for others? That is the question. Jesus did not cry for Himself. He cried for the nation of Israel, wondering what would happen to it if He were to die. He cried for the dead Lazarus. When He cried for dead Lazarus, He shed tears on behalf of all humanity in this world, who, like Lazarus, are hoping for the touch of resurrection from the power of death.

Even on the path of death, where His life was coming to an end, at the final cliff, He said, “Even if my life is extinguished, may Your will be fulfilled.” Even in the miserable and extreme situation of asking, “My God, why have You forsaken me?” He shed tears, saying, “I go for the day of Your victory; please accept my unchanging heart of devotion.” The tears of Jesus are different. That is why those who cry for themselves are doomed. Do you understand? “Yes.”

Do not cry for yourself; cry for others.
No matter how beautiful a woman is, if she gets married and tells her husband, “You promised to love me when you brought me here, so why don’t you love me? It makes me feel bad,” she should throw away her self-pity. If I want to provoke you, I should say “self-pity.” That creates a stimulus. Just saying “eyes” doesn’t create a stimulus. Do you understand? Such self-pity can be discarded on the spot.

Even when going to work in the morning, saying, “You should love me before going to work,” if there is no expression of love, that is not acceptable. That is also not allowed. Think about it, ladies. If there is a woman who says, “Oh, I’m fine. Please love your work and your country more than me,” life at home would be dull. People would say, “What kind of wife is that?” However, those who know would say, “Wow, that woman is wonderful!” Men need to understand this.

Men think that once they get married, it’s all about themselves. You all received blessings this time, right? “Yes.” Don’t you tell this deacon to only think of himself? He has talent. He has talent. Yes, right? I can see that he has talent. You can tell just by looking at his eyes and nose. (Laughter) Be careful. Everyone in the world absolutely dislikes those who cry selfishly.

When a mother shares food, no matter how much you cry for more, it won’t work. In the past, I cried a lot. I would act up to see if anyone would sympathize with me. “You should give me more. I am the best person in this house, so even if you give something good, you should give it to me first.” I would throw a tantrum. When I cried, it wasn’t just a few hours; it would last a whole day, typically. (Laughter) That’s how I would cry. After crying like that, eventually, I wouldn’t have tears left, and my nose would run, and when there’s nothing left to come out, my throat would hurt. (Laughter) My stomach would hurt, and there would be no part of me that didn’t hurt. I shouldn’t say this, but I have to. I have to speak honestly.

When I was crying like that, my sister, who had gone out to the fields in the morning, would come in around lunchtime to cook. Then I would think, “Surely my sister will come and comfort me. When she comes to comfort me, I should stop her at the first word.” I would glance to see, “That kid has such bad habits, what’s wrong with her?” (Laughter) I would be treated like a nuisance. The teacher knows well about crying. He has done a lot of research. Because I would cry for a whole day, my nickname was “Day Cry.” (Laughter)

When I cried, I didn’t just sit there and cry. I would lie down and cry until all the hair on the back of my head fell out and the skin on my heels peeled off. (Laughter) I cried like that. “Let’s see how hard I can cry, let’s cry until blood comes out.” That’s how I would cry. But even after crying like that, the response was pitiful. (Laughter) Crying for myself was utterly miserable.

Then, I would cry in the opposite way. When my older brother and younger brother would fight, you see, if there are many siblings, they will fight. And fighting is necessary for growth. Fighting is not a bad thing. If you can’t resolve the fight afterward, that’s bad, but if the environment allows for resolution, you should fight. I have fought a lot. I have many sisters. With eight siblings, it’s well organized. So, we would fight.

When my older brother and sister would fight, I would sneak off to report to my parents. I would tell them how my brother and sister fought and that my brother was bad and my sister was bad. Then my brother would come and say, “Hey, you little brat, if I did that, I would have done it, but do you have to snitch on me?” and then he would pinch and hit me. Then I would cry. It was a chance to cry. When I cried like that, I was bold. I would never lower my head. I can’t tell you how refreshing it felt. I would cry a lot. The more I cried, the more my brother would scold me. The more I cried, the more scolding I received, so they would send reinforcements. They would send another sibling to say, “Hey, go comfort your brother.” But I wouldn’t listen to that. Then my parents would come… What can you do when you keep crying? (Laughter) But even so, if that doesn’t work, then they would tell my brother to confess. So, I received confessions from my brother and sister. The thrill of that moment is unforgettable.

That is why crying for others is truly wonderful. Crying for oneself leads to frustration and misery… I can’t express that. Do you understand what I mean? Do you get it? If you cry for others, the world opens up, and everything becomes your domain. In the past, if someone didn’t want to hear crying, they would turn their heads, but when family members see someone crying like that, they would think, “That’s worth crying for. That’s worth it.” Even parents would come and say, “Hey, hey, don’t cry,” showing sympathy. This may seem simple, but it’s not. You are the same.

The fact that I have embarked on this path today may be due to “Day Cry.” Those who cry for themselves do not receive sympathy. However, those who cry for others do receive sympathy. That’s how it works. Isn’t it?

Fallen humans, you see, many people play the flute and cry for themselves. So, was Jesus aware of this?

When you go to Jerusalem, I thought the Garden of Gethsemane was deep in the mountains, a place where tigers and wolves come and go, but when I went to Jerusalem, it wasn’t like that. Do you think that’s true or not?
