It is the life of those who pursue patience. That is why among those who were persecuted and mocked in that era, there are many saints and great people. This is a historical fact.

What is the significance of the Day of Children and its mission?
So, what is the Day of Children and its mission? In the sight of God, who looks upon fallen humanity today, what kind of person is God seeking, whom does God want to meet? Is it a person like Adam and Eve, who shed tears in their fall? When considering whose tears they were, they shed the wrong tears, so now we must shed good tears, normal tears. We must become people who shed tears not for ourselves but for God, for the world, and for future generations. Adam and Eve shed tears for their own generation and sought happiness for their own generation, but they fell. However, today we must shed tears not for our own generation but for the future, for the world, and for God. Without doing that, we cannot stand before God.

When we reflect on the significance of the Day of Children today, if you want to be a child, what position should you stand in? How many tears have you shed for God? Have you ever struggled to walk the path of sacrifice, even if it means tearing your limbs, to repay God for His efforts? You haven’t. To pursue the position of “child,” you must shed such public tears. You must meet God the Father and say, “Father, when You lost Your son or our ancestors, how much sorrow filled Your heart? Also, how much humiliation, pain, and suffering have You endured throughout history through their descendants?” You must be able to shed infinite tears of sympathy. Even though God has the omnipotent authority to judge the whole world and even Satan, He stands in a position where He can’t act, unable to have the environment He should have, suffering alone, being slandered before Satan, and having all His footholds taken away by the world of Satan.
When you think about God's position, it is truly astonishing. How many tears have you shed while empathizing with God's position? The problem culminates here. When you can put aside your personal tears and shed public tears for your descendants, for the world, and for God, only then will you qualify to bear the name of a child. You must have the qualifications of a child to celebrate the Day of Children.

Now, until now, you have shed tears. Can a human being live every day only shedding tears? No, right? But what is the motivation for humans to shed tears? Just as our Unification Church principles have taught us, the motivation for shedding tears comes from wandering off on their own path of love. Isn’t that the case in the world? Even if a son or daughter is born into a prestigious family with parents and relatives, if they act recklessly, they will go wrong. No one guarantees anything for them. They will be scolded, “You’re just like that child. You did as you pleased, and now look where you are.” They will be chased away without a second thought. However, if the parents and relatives, the whole neighborhood, help them get married, and if the outcome is not good, the responsibility lies with the mother and father. When I am in sorrow, there is someone who cries for me before I do. Isn’t that so? My mother and father will cry for me first. Or perhaps uncles, cousins, and relatives will all show sympathy. So, what is wise?

That is why we must move according to principles. If you stand in a position that moves according to principles, no matter how lonely it may be, even in the most isolated position, your own fence will love you. Isn’t that right? The fence of my love protects me from the environment in proportion to my loneliness. Such a person will never fail. They will be revived. They will resurrect. And in resurrection, they will not return to a place worse than before but will rise to a better place. This is how it is viewed. It may be a lonely place, a place of sorrow, a place that seems about to break, but that is not the end. Already, there is great love residing there.

However, is there love when one acts recklessly on their own? Is there an environment of love? There is none. Even if you look around, it is desolate. Everything leads to curses and resentment; one cannot have an environment of sympathy. That is why wise people always think about an environment of sympathy and navigate accordingly. Among sympathy, of course, there is the sympathy of historical ancestors, but a wise person is one who lives with the connection to receive God’s sympathy, societal sympathy, and the sympathy of future descendants. Someone like Jesus lived that way.

Did Jesus truly love people while he was on this earth? Do you think he experienced love? Did Jesus truly love his mother and father? How would you answer if asked that? Do you think he did? Did he love his uncles, grandmothers, and grandfathers if he had them? And what about his siblings? He received scolding from his younger siblings. They would say to Jesus, “If you want to reveal yourself, why are you hiding here instead of going up to Jerusalem first?” 

For over 30 years, Jesus had a mouth but could not speak. He had eyes but could not see clearly, and he had ears but could not hear properly. Jesus lived a busy life in silence, enduring everything to pave the way for future generations. And when the time came, he set out on the road, but did he find disciples he could love? For three years, he traveled with his disciples, doing all sorts of things, but who stood by Jesus? They were just using him.

If Jesus had received their love at the cross, would he have asked them, “Do you want to be with me, or do you want me to be with you?” Looking at that, we can see through the scriptures that there were conflicting factors. When Jesus wrapped a towel around his head and poured water into a basin to wash the feet of his disciples, did he do it because he loved them? When the disciples gathered, they were just talking about who the teacher loved and whatnot, so Jesus taught them the way of serving and being served directly. From that, we can see that the disciples did not love Jesus.

Peter, James, and John, the three chief disciples, all fled later, didn’t they? You might ask why the chief disciples did not love Jesus, but look. After Jesus resurrected, he asked Peter three times, “Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?” Peter answered three times, “You know that I love you more than these.” When Jesus asked him once, twice, and three times, Peter answered three times because he was foolish. A wise and shrewd person would have bowed their head after being asked once or twice. This shows that Peter was foolish.

When Jesus asked, “Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?” it was a reminder of Peter’s three betrayals in the past. So, the fact that he stood firm and answered three times indicates that Peter was foolish. He is a person with a bear-like personality. Such a person is not wise or shrewd. When he was asked a second time, he did not say, “I have nothing to say.” Who knows? Peter might have answered, “I cannot say that,” but the fact that he could stand firm and say it three times shows that Peter was foolish. Isn’t that so?

What would you do? Even though Peter had a history of denying Jesus three times, if Jesus looked at him with piercing eyes and pointed fingers, asking, “Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?” wouldn’t you bow your head and bend your back? Would you be able to stand tall and say, “You know that I love you more than these”? Is there anyone among the men here who could do that? This shows that Peter was foolish.

Looking at this, did Jesus love his disciples? If he had appeared after his resurrection and said, “Oh, I came looking for you because of you. I came to find you because I had regrets after dying,” then perhaps we could say Jesus loved his disciples. But seeing how he reprimanded them upon meeting them, did Jesus love his disciples? He also dismissed his mother by saying, “Woman, what does that have to do with me?” Jesus came to this world and dismissed his own mother and his disciples. So, who did Jesus love? Did he love Mary Magdalene? Not at all. When Mary Magdalene approached the resurrected Jesus, he told her, “Do not touch me.” If he loved her, would he have said that? Jesus left this earth without being able to love people.

The place where God's and humanity's wishes (the standard of value) are realized  
Then, the important question arises: where will we find the standard of value that everyone desires? Moreover, what religious people desire is heaven. Their wish ultimately culminates in entering heaven and becoming a person of heaven. That is their wish. In other words, when we ask where a valuable human can stay after becoming such, the answer is heaven. We know that heaven is also structured in stages. Just as there are classes in society, and distinctions of upper, middle, and lower exist, there are also upper, middle, and lower levels in the spiritual realm. Looking at Paul's experiential account of seeing the third heaven, and also considering the biblical teachings about the glory of the sun, the glory of the moon, and the glory of the stars, we understand that there are various levels.  
Order must begin with the subject... To establish relationships, there must be an organizational order. One cannot escape from order. Order cannot be achieved without a sequence of precedence and succession. From this perspective, we can understand the hierarchy of upper, middle, and lower based on precedence, superiority and inferiority, and left and right relationships. When we consider this, there are also various levels among those who enter heaven.  
So, what determines these levels? It is a matter of value. The question of how valuable a person is can be a determining factor for that level.  
Shouldn't the standards of a more valuable human that people desire and the standards that heaven desires align? If the standards of value that heaven desires differ from those that humanity desires, then it cannot become a world that pleases heaven. When this is achieved, and both humanity and heaven can rejoice, a foundation for happiness is established.  
Happiness cannot exist in solitude. Happiness cannot be found in solitude... No matter how much authority one possesses in this world, if that authority exists in a place of loneliness, then that person is not happy.  
When one stands in the center, the broader and larger the field related to that center, the more the standard of their happiness is determined by that breadth and size. That is why we desire to possess many things. We wish to acquire more precious things. We strive to connect with more valuable things in our daily lives. Why is that? It is to encounter an environment where we can be happier.  
Thus, happiness cannot exist in a lonely and isolated place. Happiness can only exist in establishing relative relationships. Moreover, that relative relationship must be a responsive relationship, not a conflicting one. Happiness exists in establishing a relationship where both parties harmonize and care for each other.  
Even if a relative relationship exists, there can be no happiness in a place where each seeks to benefit only themselves. The more that mutual concern for each other becomes evident, the more pronounced it becomes, and the more it resonates throughout the whole, the greater the stimulation of happiness spreads to everyone. If that place becomes limited, happiness will also be restricted to that limit.  
When we consider God Himself, why did He create this vast universe? God created the vast universe not to seek happiness in a small domain but because He desired a broader realm of happiness. The Creator, who is the subject of this vast universe, and the created beings, who can never invade that position, were meant to be factors of happiness that can give and receive from each other.  
When the created beings and the Creator can correspond rather than conflict, the created beings become valuable, and when they rejoice and are happy, the Creator can also rejoice and be happy. Only in such a position can the joy beyond creation be realized.  
The standard of personality that humanity pursues  
Because God created humans according to such connections, humans themselves desire the same. How great is that desire? It is for the infinite. If there is something that pursues their relative personality, it is not a personality within the realm we can conceive. Even after thousands or tens of thousands of years, they are waiting for a personality greater than they can imagine, unknowingly. In other words, we humans are pursuing a value-laden personality that exceeds our own thoughts and the thoughts of others.  
That is why, as beings who pursue such a personality, if such humans become the subject, then the objects they desire must also be infinitely great. No matter what you possess, you cannot be satisfied with just one. Even if you make the entire world your own, there remains a desire for something beyond that world. In other words, because you are envisioning a standard of personality that cannot be pursued by your own thoughts, you cannot help but desire a relative world.  
In this light, where will the standard of human personality value be found? Can we say that the standard of value is something that appears as a specific target within a limited time or space? Of course, we can say, "This is it," but we do not want to confine it to any boundary or realm. We are hoping for a standard that acknowledges ourselves standing at the central position connected to the infinite and the vast universe. In other words, we hope to say, "This is it," not within any boundary but in a way that encompasses the whole.  
Therefore, if human desires are infinite, then the standard of personality that humans desire must also connect to the infinite. It must extend to the standard that can transcend any boundary.  
If the standard of personality expands so broadly, what could be the core that can serve as its center? You might think it is "me," but just "me" cannot be the core. Alone in the vast universe, one cannot be the center. There must be something with which one can pursue relative value. So, what is that something that can pursue relative value? It must be something like oneself. It must be similar to oneself but must possess relativity. That is why there are men and women. Both men and women must seek such a standard of value. The starting point of such value cannot exist apart from oneself.  
Then, to establish a relationship with oneself, what is the primary standard for that relationship? It must be something like oneself. Therefore, even for a person with a highly regarded standard of personality, that primary standard must ultimately be someone like themselves.  
Love binds men and women together  
In the human world, there are men and women. It is certain that both men and women are valuable beings, but where does that value derive from? Such a question is determined by centering on them and also centering on myself. So, what kind of place can be said to be the center for both of us? When we seek a place where both can be placed favorably, it cannot be a vague place that is simply good.  
So, where could that place be? If we apply the nouns we consider good today, it is a place deep within the heart. If there is goodness deep within the heart, that good place will become the center. That deep place in the heart is invisible. So, what is that deep place in the heart? It is not a place of solitude. It must be a place where both can be together. If it is such a place, then both must enter each other's hearts. It must be one, not two. So, where could that place be? The conclusion is that it must be a place of love. Therefore, among those who love each other, they seek to love deeply in their hearts, genuinely, and truly.  
When you say something is good, if you just say it is good, it lacks flavor. However, if you say, "I truly love deeply in my heart," then it has flavor. Therefore, they must break down the boundaries and bind together as one. That point of connection is not a place where they simply face each other. It is a place where they harmonize and cannot tell whether they are one or two. If such a place has emerged, what kind of place is it? It is the place where the standard of value that humanity desires aligns with the standard that heaven desires, the standard from which heaven can emerge. If this does not align in any one place, it cannot become a world of joy. There is no origin or motivation for joy there.  
So, where will it start to connect as one? Where will that point of connection be? As mentioned earlier, it is a place where he is in me, and I am in him. If you look at John 14 in the Bible, there is a saying: "I am in the Father, and the Father is in me, and you are in me, and I am in you." What is this saying centered on? When we say "truth," it is a relative concept. Everything is like that. When we say "goodness," that goodness is also a relative concept, but when we say "love," what feeling does that evoke? When we say "love," it evokes a feeling of being in sync with each other. Thus, that saying (John 14:20) is centered on love. What kind of love is it? It is a love based on the standard that God desires. It is like the leaven that breaks down the boundaries between hearts and unites them as one; it is the cause, the motivation, the essence, which is love.  
This love, if small, is exceedingly small; if great, it is exceedingly great. Among those who love, isn't it true? When a deeply loving person merely blinks their eyes or glances, it feels as if the world is turned upside down. When a loving person smiles, it feels as if the world is in turmoil. If they are sensitive, they are that sensitive; if small, they are that small; if great, they are that great; if visible, they are visible; if invisible, they are invisible... The only thing that can break those boundaries is love.  
Therefore, a loving person is occupied in their heart. Every word begins with the person they love. Isn't that true? They want to give something centered on the person they love, to receive something centered on the person they love, to whisper centered on the person they love, and to connect everything with the person they love. If they become disconnected from the person they love, then the entire universe becomes bothersome. This is something you can all understand.  
The place where humans can feel happiness  
Everything unfolds around the person they love. Happiness and unhappiness, everything unfolds around the person they love. Is that not true? Let’s consider an example from our real lives.  
There is a millionaire grandfather. From a worldly perspective, he has everything. He has children, money, power, and externally, he lacks nothing to be envied. However, if that grandfather is a lonely old man, would we say, "Ah, that old man is a happy man who can represent the world"? Think about lonely grandfathers. Probably not. Although he may not have reached that point yet, it is true. No matter how handsome or beautiful a man or woman is, if they live alone, they are pitiful. There is no need to say more about that.  
So, where does happiness begin? This is an extremely significant question. Happiness cannot manifest without a standard of value being established, and where does that standard of value begin? It cannot start from me. The standard of value cannot be established from me. It must be established between you and me, between you and me. It starts from a place where there is someone like me, where I can completely love them and be completely loved by them, a place where I can give completely and receive completely.  
When we think about this issue, even if one is trapped alone in a cave, if there is someone who can sacrifice their life for them, even while walking the path of death, if they can think of that person they love, then at that moment, they are not an unhappy person. No matter how lonely, miserable, or in a situation where life and death are intertwined, if they can overcome that place, the power to overcome all those circumstances comes from the certainty that the person they love is working hard for them and that by walking this path, they can make that person happy.  
Life and love  
In this light, what is the motive of life? Today, the philosophical community is also discussing life and existence. The question is whether existence comes first or life comes first. Without life, there can be no existence.  
So, is life first, or what comes first? Life must necessarily involve relative connections.
It must be created through necessity. Life cannot come into existence without relative relationships. Before life exists, there must be relative relationships. So, what kind of relative relationship is it? It is a relationship of love. Life comes into being through a relative love relationship. Therefore, there must be love before life exists. This is how it works.

You must have had such relative relationships in having life. What is that relative relationship? It is the love of parents. If you trace that parental relationship back, it goes all the way to Adam and Eve. What happens when you reach Adam and Eve? Even Adam and Eve, to exist with life, must have some relative relationship. There must be something that desires to love, something that is lovable and cannot help but love, a relative something that can go through that inner relationship. This relative something that can be connected is what we call God. That is why the concept of the dual characteristics of God, as spoken in the Unification Church, cannot be explained without this understanding.

The dual characteristics are not separate; they must be centered around love and must be united in an eternal oneness, establishing a standard of absolute value. This is God, who is the central subject of the dual characteristics as described in the Unification Church. That God is not just a vague being alone. He is in a position of subjectivity to achieve unity with a counterpart. So, who is in a relative position to achieve unity with that God? It is humanity.

Humanity must become completely one with God. Where is the point of union that can achieve this? In other words, where can three become one? Where can four become one? Where is the place where they can reconcile into one, where they can say, "He is me, and I am he"? When we look at this problem, we can say, "There is no greater love than to love your neighbor as yourself."

So, where is the place of that love that can love as oneself? Among men living alone, or among women living alone, God's love cannot be present. God's love comes to the place where one can be completely one, standing at the forefront of having seen the determination of perfect value centered on love. The term bride and bridegroom, as spoken by Jesus Christ, is also based on this point. When they unite in love, the love of the horizontal subject and object, man and woman, is intertwined with the vertical love of God, allowing for the establishment of a three-dimensional realm of love. Not recognizing this origin of love is what is called the Fall. This is the teaching of the Unification Church.

What should be the standard of value that humanity pursues? 

When we look at this, what should the standard of human value be? Is it knowledge? When I say I love someone, do I love them because they have a master's degree or a doctorate? When it comes to love, all those things disappear. In love, those things are not needed at all. It is about loving the person themselves. Their eyes are better than knowledge, and their appearance is better than knowledge. The person themselves is better than anything else. That is how it should be. That position is a more valuable standard than what is demanded in the relative world, such as knowledge or power. Therefore, the place where anything other than that person is visible is not the place of true love. Marrying for money, marrying for power, marrying for knowledge is not true love. Knowledge cannot stand before love, power cannot stand before love, and money cannot stand before love. In a direct relationship, love must come first.

When we consider this issue, what should the standard of human value be? Without love, a standard of value cannot be established. The term love exists within the realm of relative concepts, so each person's standard of value is also established within that realm. To what extent can that core, where the subject and object can unite through the principles of creation, be...

If there is a vertical line that heaven looks upon, the core where that vertical line can rest is a single point. This is similar to hanging a tree; if it is centered perfectly, it will balance at that point. If it tilts, it becomes a serious problem. If it tilts, the whole thing starts to misalign. However, if it is centered on the vertical line, it can maintain equilibrium. There must be such a place. There must be, right? Humans may not know it, but there must be such a place.

God's love is absolute and unchanging, so it is a single path. It is a path that goes only one way. Therefore, it can achieve unity centered on the vertical. That unity occurs when man and woman love each other. If they are a couple, this refers to the ancient Adam and Eve. They must unite in love. That point of union must not lean to one side. There must be a place where three points stick together perfectly on the vertical line. What would have happened if ancient Adam and Eve had stood in such a place? If that were the case, God would not need much power. If that were the case, there would be no need for actions to generate new strength. Because they are already united, even a slight movement can affect the whole. If the two raise themselves just a little, the whole rises, and if they lower themselves just a little, the whole descends. If they widen, they rise, and if they narrow, they descend. However, if it tilts, the whole thing becomes misaligned. Isn’t there a standard where that vertical line and the flat center can meet?

That would be the standard of value that God sees in relation to humanity. There must be such a standard of value. It is neither knowledge nor power. It is not external. One can feel as if they possess everything just by being themselves and can say they do not want anything else. After having that, after achieving that, to adapt a more joyful relationship to the whole, and to expand another world of relative impressions, something else may be needed, but the primary condition is that. Thus, a man seeks a woman, and a woman seeks a man. Isn’t that right? That is undoubtedly true in the human world.

It is centered around Adam and Eve. Adam goes out to find a woman, and Eve goes out to find a man. When Adam goes out to find Eve, does he seek her centered on Eve? No. He seeks her centered on God. He looks for her while focusing on God. Likewise, when Eve goes out to find Adam, she does not seek him centered on Adam but seeks him centered on God. In other words, they seek each other from a relative position centered on God's vertical line. They are looking for the place where three points meet. Therefore, the standard of personality, the standard of value, begins from the point of love that centers on God. You must understand that this is an undeniable principle. This is the primary standard.

To love the world, first love people.

So, what should fallen humanity hope for from each other? They must hope for God and hope for God's love. If God's love is vertical, then they must seek men or women centered on that vertical line. When a person stands here—there is only one animal that walks upright, and that is a human. Only then can they develop. That becomes a day, a year, ten years, or even a lifetime until they die. There must be something like that. That is why history seeks direction. History has not found direction until now. Therefore, it is seeking that direction.

Then, what is the representative center in loving a country? In loving the world, who should I love first? I must love individuals first. How should I love individuals? Of course, if a man loves another man, it is love centered on some purpose. It is love pursued for some result; there is nothing else. Do men love each other? That is because their intentions align. That is how friendships are formed. They love each other from the perspective of a common purpose. The same goes for women loving each other; it is love centered around some purpose. If that purpose does not exist, there is no love. They do not even like each other. However, when it comes to men and women loving each other, it is not love centered on any purpose. They love each other without any purpose. Therefore, it is seen as motivated love.

From this perspective, in loving the world, to truly love the world, one must first truly love people. To truly love people, one must truly love their counterpart. The mother and father love in that way. If they loved like that, and if Eve had not fallen, the love of those parents would have become absolute love. They would have entered into the realm of absolute love. Why? Because they entered into a relative position that can connect with the absolute love of God, which is vertical, they entered into the realm of relative love that can unite with the absolute, thus becoming absolute themselves. Isn’t that so? If a woman marries well, she can jump into the position of her husband's authority without any merit. Isn’t that right? There is a method that can occupy in a leap in the world of love.

When we look at it this way, if one receives God's love, the kingdom of heaven is direct. It can directly access the value realm of the whole and can prevent interference from becoming a problem in the world of love.

To come into existence, there must be parents. Is it enough to just have parents? No. There must be a counterpart. Without a counterpart, it becomes the end forever.

I do not only love my father.

Education in God's Love

Sometimes I would fall while climbing and hang on to a branch, dangling there. God bless! If I die, it would be a big deal. (laughter) 

In front of our house, there was a big tree. It was quite large, and there was a magpie nest there. Ah, this magpie laid eggs, and I was curious about it every day. That is the teacher's character. Until I found out for sure, I couldn't sleep at night. (laughter) The night before, I went up to check, and early in the morning, before the magpie came out, I would sneak up to see. When I went up, it laid one egg, then two eggs, then three eggs, and every day the number of eggs increased. Because I kept going up and down, I became friends with the magpie. At first, it would screech and make a fuss, but since I kept coming up every day, it didn’t mind and just stayed there. (laughter) So I observed everything about how it fed its chicks and what it did.

Whenever a new bird appeared, I caught all of them. There was no bird I hadn’t caught. If there was a unique bird, I would stay up all night for several days to guard it. Now, I earnestly hope that we can become a group of unification that can awaken the path of this sleeping nation, unify the division of the North and South, and prepare ourselves as the heralds of tomorrow's hope.

Please fulfill your will and bring about your day of safety and victory through our humble and earnest tears. I earnestly ask and wish that you would solidify it through our hard work and sweat.

We have understood how precious the mission and responsibility of the headquarters are. As we reflect on ourselves, we present everything before you and receive new commands, becoming heavenly sons and daughters who have no shame as we start a vigorous tomorrow.

Until we meet again, may you protect us. I pray in the name of our parents. Amen.
Though it seems like a single place, when we think of it as a foundation where the deep currents of the heart intersect and reveal their connections to one another, it appears to be nothing at all. Yet, it is a bond that even the world cannot alter, a bond that even heaven cannot change, and a place that cannot be affected by the authority of the Absolute. When we reflect on the fact that this place can only be exercised, moved, and established through love, we come to realize the nobility of a parent's love and the preciousness of a parent's heart that longs for their child.

O Father, who resides high in heaven! I try to grasp the pure heart of the Father, who wishes to take all people in the most humble of positions as His children. When I think about who will initiate the love that You desire and long for, I come to understand that it will be through the son whom You cannot forget and through the daughter whom You will begin with.

When viewed through the lens of historical eras, You have a pure, noble, and clean heart, forgetting all that is Yours as You long to love the true sons and daughters who have replaced the value of Your entire being with the longing of Your heart. The central sons and daughters, who can symbolize Your joy, who You want to see again and again, who You wish to speak with eternally, and who You want to keep with You forever, are Your noble sons and daughters. They appear as a single body, more limited than the infinite, manifesting as a solitary existence, even if they cannot represent the entirety. When I reflect once more on how much You have desired to embrace and love these sons and daughters in a place where tears well up in Your eyes, I cannot help but think of how much You must have longed for this.

If You could not do so, then because You are the master of heart and love, You must feel more sorrow than anyone else, more regret than anyone else, and more heartache than anyone else. As I think about this, I become acutely aware of the wrongs committed by our ancestors during the historical era.

O Father, in front of the heart of the Father who came with such wishes, our ancestors fell into the path of corruption that they did not desire. They became a shameful sight before You, unable to show their faces in front of Your voice calling them with love, and they became anxious in the presence of Your kind words. When I think about the moment of that corruption, how incredibly dreadful and loathsome that time and day must have been, I realize that it was a day that neither You nor the sons wanted, bringing forth the results of the fall.

Carrying the burden of sin and wandering the lonely path of exile for thousands of years, feeling the emotions that change with the seasons, whether it rains or snows or the wind blows, I must take responsibility for my own shortcomings while passing through the historical era, and I must seek connections before You with tears of repentance. Yet, I feel how miserable the heart of the Father must be as He looks upon humanity struggling in a position where they do not even know how they have become.

If there are sons and daughters who cry out for me to find them, I know that we must atone for the historical connections that cannot face You before they cry out. When I think about Your will, which cannot escape reality, and when I ponder how many of the heavenly lineage are struggling to remove the factors that do not please You from this world, longing for a form that can bring You joy among the 3 billion people on this earth, I wonder if there are truly sons and daughters in the true sense. When I consider how our lives as humble humans are, and how we are struggling through the course of life centered on our hearts, I cannot help but feel that You, who seek the standard of complete truth, are indeed a pitiful Father, and I cannot help but feel how lamentable it is that we are in such a situation.

When I realize that this hand, this body, or even our entire senses and emotions are not connected to You but rather to the enemy Satan, increasing the path of sorrow before You, I must recognize that I am in a position that is shameful before You, both in front and behind. 

We, who are in such a position, have been cast out from the heavenly kingdom to a place lower than the servants of heaven, and it is only natural that we should stand in a position of wearing a prison uniform, carrying the sorrow of a thousand years, and seeking the virtue You have bestowed upon us with tears of repentance. However, the path of the connection of our original nature, which we must seek, cannot disappear as long as You exist.

When we think about the position of the prodigal son, it is natural to seek out our parents when we are lonely, and when we feel more miserable than anyone else, it is the bond with our parents and the longing for their embrace that is human nature. We feel that no matter how vast the universe may be, we have no land on which we can stand, and the more beautiful the myriad of things we see, the more we realize our shameful selves. Even though there may be countless humans, we find ourselves in a lonely position, feeling that those many humans are greater and more admirable than ourselves.

However, when we consider that the flowing heart of our original nature is deeply yearning to find our heavenly parents, I believe that there have been many religious individuals who have struggled in such a position in the past, and many groups seeking truth. But how many people lived without knowing that there is a Being who thinks of them in such a way and has such a connection? O Father, yet only we of the Unification Church, only we who bear the name of Unification Church members, know this. We know this fact.

For the value of infinite life, there are groups who stand at the crossroads of fighting against death with the pain of their own bodies, pledging to walk the path of true life’s victory, and there are those seeking true life. Even if there are those who wish to become victorious, it is only natural to know that humanity cannot do it alone. When we see that humans cannot solve everything by themselves, we cannot help but feel that they are powerless and unable to take responsibility for the whole from the position of the subject. Therefore, if it is said that humanity's fate is to fall into a deep valley and look up at the high mountain, then we must realize that the more treacherous the path we must climb, the more miserable our fate becomes.

What we should hope for is not only our own strength but also the existence of another source of strength. It is certain that there must be a place to long for and hope for, and we have come to know that the One who has appeared in place of that is God. To hold onto that God… just as one must have faith that they can cross all the treacherous mountains and valleys in the process of looking toward the peak, we must have a heart that desires to conquer that peak and a faith stronger than the belief that we can overcome the treacherous mountains we see before us; otherwise, we cannot grasp heaven in our lives.

In such a position, if we cannot call upon our beloved parents, beloved siblings, beloved relatives, beloved spouses, beloved sovereigns, and beloved leaders of the world, then we must realize that there is no way for You to come to us.

O Father, how wonderful it would be if this place, where the little children have gathered, could become a place that passes through the quiet and deep night and welcomes the morning of creation that can forge new connections! If there is a new movement of strength here, let it be the power that comes from You, and if a new connection is being born, let us know that it is the point of birth that is realized based on You. If I can be wrapped up in that point, if I can be moved by it, and if I can become a relative reality, how blessed and desired that position must be; we must recognize this.

O Father, we must know that we are to stand in a position where we have no way to hide our shame, carrying the sorrow of a thousand years before You, and as we call out Your name a thousand or ten thousand times from the depths of our hearts, we must become those who feel ashamed after saying “Father.”

Sometimes, I remember the words You spoke. A parent who comes to find a lonely child is lonelier still. O Father, that is true. A parent who has lost a child, who has lost a son, even if they stand as the most authoritative person on earth, in a position admired by all humanity, will shed tears and struggle to find their child, disregarding their own dignity and face. I realize that a parent who loses a child loses not only their son or daughter at once but also loses everything they longed for in an instant. With the sorrow of a thousand years, along with the suffering of countless eons, facing the wall of death, standing before the standard of the Father who looks upon the path of historical restoration that cannot be solved alone, if the pitch-black darkness has been obscured from the Father’s wishes, there could not have been a greater darkness, and if the cliff has been obscured, there could not have been a greater cliff; we did not know the circumstances of the Father.

O Father, as I stand here, if there is sorrow in Your heart, please allow me to feel Your sorrow to the point of soaking my chest. If there is pain in You, please allow me to feel Your pain. This is what I have come to hope for. How many shameful things have there been before You…

In the path that the Unification Church has traversed, along with this nation and humanity…
I know well how many paths of resentment have been left behind. Thinking about the fact that there are no sons and daughters on this earth who can love you, and considering that there is no one who carries the responsibility to teach others about you as such a person, I have held onto the Unification Church and come this far.

Father, from the day I discovered that I cannot think of boasting about myself while envisioning a glorious day, from the moment I realized that I must know your sorrowful path and take it on your behalf, from the time I could understand that your place is a lonely one, and from the moment I recognized that you are the embodiment of love who comes forth in place of the death that is exchanged on the path of death, my concern has been how to follow you correctly.

Father, what has the Unification Church left before this society today, and what offerings do we have in our hearts? As an offering that we can boast about, I have received it on this foundation, and even if it costs us our lives, we must leave this behind for all people, for this nation, and for our descendants. When I think that without a group that is determined to leave this behind even if I die, the purpose cannot be fulfilled, I must feel once again how foolish our past endeavors for the purpose were and how shameless our position is in following the purpose.

Father, today is December 5, 1971, the first Sabbath of the last month of 1971. I believe that lonely daughters and sons scattered across the Korean Peninsula are gathering, calling your name in a shabby manner. If their purpose in gathering is for themselves, if they become a group that gathers to receive blessings for themselves, they will perish. They must gather for this nation, for the world, and for you.

We know that all our senses and all our perceptions must be felt in a position where they can return to you and conclude in you, and that this must become the norm for us gathered today. Therefore, I earnestly hope and wish that you will protect this day.

Please protect the Republic of Korea, Father. Please safeguard this pitiful nation, which has a foolish relationship that cannot be without your love. Among them, the most pitiful group is the group of unification gathered here. I know that we must not only offer their blood and flesh before you but also before this nation. However, I recognize that they are an insufficient group that has not become the holy people, so Father, please nurture them. I earnestly hope and wish that you will take care of them for the time being.

Furthermore, please remember the blessed families. Many young lives have grown up among them, having inherited the purpose, so Father, please look upon them with compassion. Their suffering and their inadequate positions are for this nation and for the world, so Father, please protect them. I earnestly ask that you allow them to establish families that you can take pride in, where children can grow up, and grant them the living environment where they can serve you in a place that brings you joy.

Father, please protect this headquarters. When I leave on my journey, I think that the spiritual world will also try to follow that path, so this place, which must fulfill the central mission of the entire Republic of Korea, must not be lonely. At this time, let not the workers of unification become a pitiful group that loses the precious moment of holding hands and meeting together, but rather let them increase their sincerity.

You love the Unification Church because you have a purpose, and your sons and daughters boast of your purpose because they have a desire to follow that purpose. Therefore, I earnestly hope and wish that you will take charge of them. We must not become a group that is driven before our enemies. We, who stand before our enemies, must always present the conditions for victory that can subdue evil by bringing you to our side, and we must become a group that clearly realizes that this is the factor that can achieve absolute victory and the secret that can allow you to dwell here.

Father, may this day be blessed. May the remaining days of this month be blessed. We are marking 1972 as the limit of our three-year course, so please let the day come soon when we can digest the foundation of resentment that is divided by the 38th parallel under your dominion. I earnestly ask that you take charge of everything.

As we pass through the 1970s into the 1980s, for the day when your glory can shine brightly throughout the world, I earnestly ask that you encourage and inspire us to become warriors who can prepare ourselves as heavenly soldiers and strive toward the fierce battlefield. May you accomplish everything according to your will. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We see various figures around us, including the poor and those who are not. There are individuals like that, families like that, and we see neighborhoods and regions like that. Furthermore, while there are nations that are perishing, there are also nations that are thriving. We see people who are doing well and those who are not. We know that there are people who live happily and those who live in sorrow. We are well aware that this is the world we live in, filled with such contrasting environments.

However, no one draws a picture of a sorrowful life. No one wishes to walk the path of suffering. No one envisions a lonely environment. Everyone desires to be with others rather than to be alone. They seek joy and wish to find a glorious position while hoping to stand higher than others, which we can understand through our lives and our own hearts.

Because people are like this, the family, which is the most fundamental basis for human existence, is also like this. Any social organization strives to stand in such a position. Nations fight to avoid the place of sorrow and pursue a glorious position. Furthermore, we understand that the world itself is also pursuing such things.

If there is something greater and higher than the world, if there is something larger than this earth, and if there exists a being like a person, then that being must also be tracing the path of desire that humans wish for. This is something anyone would affirm.

If there is a central being that governs such people, it is only natural that this being does not wish to experience sorrowful days. This being also desires the highest position where victory and glory can reign over all creation. That highest position is not one paired with danger, loneliness, or sorrow; rather, it seeks a position where it can connect with the whole.

In other words, if God exists, then God is like us humans. If God has a heart that loves humanity, it is only natural that this loving heart does not want to love from a lonely and painful position. It is undeniable that God seeks the path of love in a place where freedom and peace dwell, and where all beings can praise that love in glory.

If there are people whom God can love, then God wishes to love in an environment of freedom, in the original place of peaceful heaven. What kind of love would God want to express? Wouldn't it be the greatest love? If that greatest love is realized, wouldn't heaven and earth bow before that love?

Where would be the place where such an individual can be found to love? And what kind of individual would that be? We must ponder this quietly.

Loving such an individual does not end there. If there is glory in the individual, the desire is not to conclude it as the individual's glory, but rather to continue it into a more developed and higher glory. When we see that humans have the desire to pursue such a higher glory, if God has loved the individual centered on that love and rejoiced, then that joy would not end there; rather, it would seek a family where love can be expanded to a higher dimension and broader environment.

Thus, in loving that family, one would not love in a lesser way than the individual. If there are ten people in that family, the desire would be to love each individual with a deeper love than the love given to one person. This is the position of the subject of love. This is something we can also anticipate through our humanity; if God stands in such a position, then the absolute love for the first person would be pursued to be absolute before the whole. It is certain that God will seek something of a higher dimension than before.

For example, if there is a person like a wife whom God loves, that love for the wife does not end there. If there is love for the wife, then God would also want to love the children. 

Would the love for the children be lower than the love for the wife? No, it would not. The love for the children does not exclude the love experienced with the wife; rather, it seeks to amplify that love with the nature of the stimulating love felt for the wife. The position of loving the children is not lesser than the serious position of loving the wife. If there is a desire for love, then one would seek to love from a more serious position, a deeper position, pursuing a more valuable content of love.

Therefore, if one loves one person among ten and then loves two more, it is not about excluding the connection of love for the two people to love three. One must have the desire to love three based on the love connection for the two. Similarly, it is not about excluding the love connection for the three to love four; rather, one must love four based on the total love experienced for the three. One must combine the love for four to love all ten.

If that is possible, would it be an unhappy situation? Would it be a painful position for the one who loves, or a position that cannot be? If there is a way to do so, anyone would want to find a position where they can love ten rather than just one. This is a conclusion we can draw based on human desire.

If there is such a family, there must also be a tribe centered around that family. Because I loved my family in this way, when I love a family centered around that love, it becomes the true way to love the tribe. It is not about excluding all the factors of love experienced through one's own family; rather, it is about wanting to love the tribe based on that.

If one has loved the tribe, then when loving the nation, it is not about excluding the factors of love for the tribe; rather, it is about seeking to love the nation by adding to the love for the tribe. Only then does it become a way to love centered around the standards of the nation and the state. And if one understands that this is a nation and a state that must eternally remain in the world, then when loving the world, one cannot love without the foundation of loving the nation.

One wants to love the world based on the love for the nation. If one wishes to love the world with a love that is less than the love for the nation, it would contradict the law of love. In this light, if a person who loves a nation wishes to love the world, they would want to love with the experience and all the factors of love they have felt for the nation, seeking to love with something greater.

When we consider this standard, we find that humans have a nature that desires to seek the world and love the world even more than the nation. From this, we conclude that we must stand in a position where we love the world more than the nation. Shouldn't it be so?

If there is a God who governs the world, then is there a position where humans can love God by separating their love for the world? Is there a position where they can love God more than the world, using their love for the world as a leaven, a foundation? If so, what position would God seek? Would God seek a position where humans can love God more than the world, or not? It goes without saying that God would seek a position where humans can love Him more than the world. This is the ultimate destination of God's desire for love.

Parents who have raised many children exhibit a broad and deep heart of love. Those who have raised many children become aware that they cannot strike down even a wicked enemy. Why? Because they stand on a broad foundation and possess a wide law.

God is the subject of the highest love. In establishing a relationship with the God who is the subject of love, it is easy to think that it is sufficient for God and me to love each other, excluding all the love for individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. Would God desire that? Would God want to center everything around just me? If God is a parent, He must have a heart of fairness and a desire to distribute love collectively from a subjective position. Thus, if there are ten people, wouldn't God be in the position of a parent to all ten?

In this light, God would not want to be loved only by me while excluding the world. He desires to be loved together with the world. He does not wish for only the Republic of Korea to receive love. He wants to receive love along with the world, beyond the concept of the Republic of Korea. To say, "Love only me," and to wish for only my love is something God does not fundamentally desire.

That is why Jesus taught, "Do not worry about what you will eat, what you will wear, or what you will drink. These are what the Gentiles seek. First, seek His kingdom and His righteousness." He did not teach to prioritize individuals or families first. He taught to seek His kingdom and His righteousness first.
(義) means that it is not something we individuals should possess, but rather something God should possess first. Therefore, if God has desires, those desires are for His kingdom and for establishing righteousness in His kingdom. Joy can only be established on the foundation of fulfilling that desire; without desires and aspirations, there can be no joy. This is a natural statement.

For this reason, when a person seeks to live for themselves, or to do well for themselves, even if they succeed, those who hold such thoughts will ultimately fail. Even if they have succeeded, if there are those who think, "I have succeeded because of them," they cannot fail along with them. When they wish to prosper together with others, they will not fail until those others fail. However, if they do fail together with them, it means that God's will has been lost. As long as God's will remains with them, if I am with them, I stand in a position where I do not fail.

For this reason, people have not established ethics and morality by advocating for a self-centered life. When speaking of public and private (公私), we first mention the public (公) and do not speak of the private (私) first. We do not say private and public (私公). The subordinate cannot be the principal. The public (公) is established in the recognition of relative rights for the sake of the whole, for the sake of you all. Where relative rights are not recognized, the private (私) is determined. Relative rights are where the public (公) exists. Where the public (公) exists, there are "you all."

What "you all" desire is not personal desire but collective desire. A place of joy centered around the collective desire cannot be swayed by individual sorrow. If a feast is held, and the environment is filled with joy centered around that feast, even if there is individual sorrow among them, saying "I am sad," no matter how much noise they make, it will be eliminated. Therefore, when a joyful day arrives, one should move in accordance with the joy of all people and stand in a position where they can stimulate joy. If someone reduces that joy, they will be expelled. Only those who can inspire and stimulate joy can leave a lasting subjectivity. When viewed this way, what kind of being is God? He is a public being.

Wise people
Now, there is the phrase "victory and defeat" here. What does victory (勝) refer to? From the perspective mentioned earlier, it does not refer to a self-centered victory. To pledge victory centered on oneself may be necessary within the boundaries of the individual, but it has nothing to do with the whole. Therefore, wise people consider the future.

What kind of day is the future? The future is a day filled with hope. A day filled with hope is not filled with personal hope but with collective hope. For this reason, those who have hope must lead a wise life. Moreover, those who possess hope lead a wise life. What is a wise life? It is not living for the sake of current victory, even though current victory is important; it is the person who strives to achieve future victory that is wise. What this means is that it does not demand a victory centered on a limited individual in the current environment, but rather a victory related to the whole.

That is, it demands a public victory. That public nature is to be whole. Therefore, goodness (善) cannot be established on a private standard. It can only be established on a public standard. Goodness (善) is achieved in a position that relates to the whole, and because it must be given and received in a position that relates to the whole, if I am in a position to face ten people, I must represent those ten people. I must be the counterpart for those ten people. If I have a hundred people as a public target, I must represent those hundred people. I must be the counterpart before those hundred people.

True victory
Whether it is a nation or a people, when one stands on a public stage centered on the Republic of Korea and says, "I will live publicly. I will love my country and my people," it aligns the direction with the whole of the Republic of Korea. The possibility of universalizing the sentiment that "you are me and I am you" can only arise from such a position, and that is where the true connection of a patriot who loves the country emerges.

Therefore, when one proclaims victory, if that victory is seen as a personal victory… if an individual has succeeded, they are only happy for themselves. If one is happy centered on the goals they desired, it is extremely one-sided. The more it expands to 360 degrees, the more it becomes distant, and the smaller it becomes. It is a victory within a very limited domain. That victory cannot relate to or influence the 360 degrees. It is a victory that cannot surpass the degrees of the left and right centered on oneself.

One can become a unit that can form two, so one can come into contact with two. Two can become a unit that can form three, so they can come into contact with three. However, personal victory is not a unit of this position; it is a limited unit. Because it is a unit centered on "me," it ultimately ends with "me." It cannot establish a relationship with the whole.

However, even if I achieve a personal victory, if I do not manage it for myself but share it with the whole, I can publicize that personal victory. What does that mean? It is the path of sacrifice. The path of sacrifice becomes the foundation that can connect the secret of another victory to the reality stage. For this reason, God, being a wise subject, teaches those who walk the path of the way (道) to sacrifice themselves. That makes sense.

Therefore, rather than respecting what is mine as mine, I must place what I respect for the sake of the whole in a position of sacrifice. Such sacrifice must be made. To become public (公), one cannot center on private (私) standards; without going through the process of sacrifice, the public cannot emerge. Therefore, the path of the way (道) is essentially the path of sacrifice. This can be seen.

If one does not know what the way is, but dedicates themselves for the country, making all kinds of sacrifices, with the mindset that before I can be happy, the Republic of Korea must be happy, and that I cannot smile until the thirty million citizens smile, let us consider a person who lives their life with such a mindset. That person's face has never smiled. It is unpleasant, ugly, and distorted. They have lived with a frown. What is the wish hidden behind that frown? No matter how ugly their appearance may be, what is the wish they hold? If their face is contorted while longing for the day when all citizens of the Republic of Korea can be happy, the more unpleasant that face becomes, the more it reveals a face that can be liked by the citizens of the Republic of Korea. The more that appearance is ugly, the more valuable it becomes. Isn't that so? The more miserable it is, the more valuable it is. There is such a path.

Loving the country with a healthy body with limbs is less valuable than becoming a cripple without legs, arms, or eyes, and loving the country. If all the motives for becoming such a being were not for oneself but for the country, then the more miserable that appearance is, the more it can become the foundation that can completely grasp the patriotic spirit of the Republic of Korea. Therefore, the path of love is the path that is prepared for sacrifice. That is the rightful path.

The path of victory cannot be achieved through means and methods. One cannot find the path of victory without being prepared for sacrifice in a sincere and serious position. Even if one claims victory through means and methods, they will be eliminated. If there is someone more serious than oneself, that serious person must inherit it. Even if one praises their own victory, they must pass it on.

If they pass it on, will they not encounter sorrow? When we consider this, what kind of victory do we desire? Is my personal victory precious? Is family victory precious? While that is precious, it cannot be boasted about to the neighborhood. When you ask the people in your neighborhood or the families in your neighborhood to "praise our family's joyful victory," if that victory has nothing to do with the neighborhood, they will not only not praise it but will laugh at it. However, if that family's victory has even a little connection with the neighborhood, the neighborhood people will say, "We praise it." Moreover, if that victory was determined with a desperate inner connection, the other party will also rejoice with a desperate heart. We can infer such things from observing our surroundings. Therefore, those who proclaim personal victory are extremely foolish.

Jesus in a public position
Look. Jesus came to this earth as a young man in his thirties and said, "I am the Son of God. I am the only begotten Son of God." From an individual standpoint, that sounds like individualism. When one thinks of "I am the only begotten," they might wonder, "Where is there a more individualistic person than that? Why are you the only one who is the only begotten?"

However, the position from which Jesus spoke such words is different from that of a human. Jesus knew more than anyone that He was the subject of God, and He knew that God was the subject of public love, and He knew that God was looking for a son who could represent the world. He understood that this son must possess such essence and such conditions.

To become a subject who can realize and fulfill that understanding, one must love the country and, furthermore, love the world, even if it means sacrificing their own life. They must become a person who can love the world even at the cost of their own life.

Standing in that self-aware position, He asked, "Isn't the son You are looking for like this?" That son is a symbol of love representing the world, a representation, a subject. That subject is the public center that God desires and the public center that all people long for. Therefore, in that position where He felt this, when He declared, "I am the only begotten Son of God," it was a profoundly public position. Thus, Jesus could even give up His life to establish the authority of the only begotten. We can see that He devoted all His thoughts to establishing the integrity of the love of the only begotten, boldly pushing forward through the path of suffering surrounded by circumstances.

For this reason, even though He died alone in a more public position, He did not die alone. The place where He died was not a place of solitary ruin but a place that could receive love from both the heavenly world and the human world, that is, a place that could bear witness to receiving God's love and human love. Because such an inner connection was formed, God's love must be manifested here, and human love must be manifested here. Therefore, wherever the name of Jesus goes, God's love is manifested, and human love is manifested. Thus, God's love and human love became intertwined, leading to the establishment of a new Christianity. At first glance, one might think Jesus was an individualist, but He was a person who stood in a more public position.

Have higher hopes and higher thoughts
The person leading the Unification Church is the same. I myself am the same. What do I live for? Do I live for food, for clothing, for a house? I do not live for those things. Then do I live for the Unification Church? I do not live for the Unification Church either. What do I live for? I do not live only for the Unification Church. I must love the country more than the Unification Church. That is the public path and the progressive path.

Those who love their family more than themselves become the masters of their family. Family members do not demand that one family member love only them. They demand a family member who loves the whole family more than themselves. Therefore, one must sacrifice themselves to save the family. One cannot love the individual that must be sacrificed in front of the family. Even if the individual sacrifices themselves, they must love the family. That is the path of goodness (善) and the stage of public progress.

How does goodness (善) develop? Goodness does not develop from loving individuals more. For an individual to be good (善), the body must not follow the desires of the mind. The mind must be centered, and the body must be willing to sacrifice; only then can the individual itself be loved. Where there is no sacrifice, especially for our fallen humanity, there is no way to be loved without increasing the conditions of sacrifice.
