It is because of the sin of not recognizing those who should be recognized.

What will mend the tattered mental attitude of this nation? There must be a needle and thread. With that needle and thread, we must sew up everything that is rotten. We must break through. Even if we go out, our identity must not change. Even if it is stained with blood and rust, that identity must not change. It must not be bent.

Then, when a person with the name of a Unification Church warrior is made a leader, will he necessarily become a needle that does not rot? This is what your leader is thinking. If you cannot be such a needle, then be the thread. The thread follows where the needle sews, right? If you cannot be a needle, I will be the needle, so you be the thread. Be the white thread. If the hand of a loyal subject is injured and cannot sew, then the dirty and rotten must be sewn with the evil thread. If there are no loyal subjects, we must educate the evil people again to make loyal subjects, right? This is the current mission of the Unification Church. You must understand this.

Current pressing issues
No matter how much the Unification Church has won, if the Republic of Korea falls, there will be nowhere to go. Therefore, we must defend the present. The communists, centered on the ideology of communism, gather around a single sovereign in an oppressive, fearful, and coercive manner, threatening life, but we, from the opposite position, must secure a practical foundation that can surpass them in practicing what we have pledged and resolved freely. This is the problem we currently face.

First, we must defend the national defense line and establish a national defense line... There are also your denominations, tribes, families, and individuals. If this defense line collapses, everything will break apart. If that happens, the Unification Church will be the first to be attacked, right? You must understand this. Currently, we have no weapons. We are completely bare. We must go out with the heart of David standing before Goliath.

At this time, to whom did God give the responsibility? To the established church or the Unification Church? As far as I know, the Unification Church has undoubtedly received that directive. But what will we use to be responsible? We have nothing. How can we make God stand before us, the Lord of Hosts, the Sovereign of Victory, and the true leader, with a sincere heart to deal with the nation on our behalf? If God reigns here and takes responsibility, we will not perish.

Whether God will allow us to strike a decisive blow against the enemy representing this denomination or not, that is the issue that will determine victory or defeat at this current point. It is a serious matter. That is why we have been praying for this nation and this people for four years. The teacher has been living with a set period for restoration providence until 1972. The providential fortune that must determine the victory or defeat of the Unification family has come before our eyes, centered on the time when Kim Il-sung turns 60.

At this moment, when a front line that has only appeared once in history is approaching us, where is the emotional feeling of a man with the spirit of a warrior, feeling the young blood pulsing through his heart? The so-called Unification Church warriors, who have kicked away the direction of decadence and corruption and stand in the position of certain victory from the direction of heavenly fortune, are you in a position to inherit such a stance or not? You must critically examine this mercilessly and coldly. Why do your eyes blink, and what is the reason for your breathing through your nose? Why do your fingers and your entire body move? What is the reason for eating and living? Where do you root the origin of life? You must analyze and critique the fundamentals.

Here, where the fate of this nation can be determined, how can you discover the self that can make a resolution and conviction to affirm the day of victory along with the national fortune that should not suffer the sorrow of defeat? This is a significant issue that the youth of the Unification Church must decide. Are you being drawn by a few bucks...? You! You miserable child, following the bowl of food for a day, dragging your mouth for something to eat, you child, you girl! It cannot be like that. It cannot be! The remaining tradition is too serious for it to be like that.

Overcome the present
Recently, some people say, "Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is a patriot." I am not someone who likes to hear such words. I am not a patriot. A patriot who can sing praises in a place where 30 million people are facing death and sorrow is not a patriot. Only when one stands in a position where they can be praised as a patriot within the realm of victory can they be a loyal subject who has fulfilled their responsibilities before the king.

I have not reached that position. I am a miserable person. When you look at the teacher here, the teacher is a miserable person. If someone says, "Your heart is like this, right?" I always live with the feeling of wanting to pour out a thousand years of sorrow. No one knows. I am a person who is thinking about what kind of person from which country I will meet. I have not yet met such a person.

Those of you centered around the headquarters have a heart that thinks of the teacher and a heart that cares for the teacher, but you must first have a heart that cares for the Republic of Korea, for the world, and for God. I do not need you to worry about me. I am a person who is walking my own path without your concern. Even if I die, I can now walk my own path. However, can you not walk your own path even if you die? Therefore, you should love the Republic of Korea more than worrying about the teacher, love humanity more than that, and love God more than that. Then love the teacher. This is your path.

When you miss the teacher, turn that heart around and long for the people of the Republic of Korea. I long for someone who can hold onto a pine tree or a blade of grass on the mountains of the Korean Peninsula and weep in place of the teacher. If that happens, that group will not perish. They will never perish. They will not perish because I have not perished. I have faced death dozens of times but have not perished or died, so if you have such a heart, you will not perish or die. It is an astonishing game.

We are in a time of tension, a time when we do not know how anxious we are. God has given me a three-year period. In that period, it was not that I did not take responsibility, but that this nation did not take responsibility, and our Unification Church did not take responsibility. If such an environment had arisen three years ago, it would not have been like this, but who would have thought that these three years would become a problem... Therefore, you must understand that it is time to make every effort to fulfill what we could not do before this day came.

We cannot perish. What should we do with the present? If we retreat, we will perish. We must overcome and surpass this. Overcoming is not just about getting over it. It is not the responsibility to just get over it; it is the responsibility to fight as we get over it.

We must overcome the present. We must overcome what we want to see, what we want to eat, and what we want to do. Only the path to victory remains for the one issue. If you think of a difficult problem as difficult here, you will perish and die. You will die. You will perish. Therefore, you must understand that you are in a position to invest everything here and resolve to overcome reality.

That is why our Unification Church needs money, talents, and strength. No one will bring these things, so we must make all preparations for reinforcement within ourselves. You must know this, and even if the teacher is not here in the future, in place of the teacher... While the teacher was in Korea, while the teacher was at the headquarters, the members of the Unification Church across the nation could think of the headquarters as a place of hope, but now that the teacher is going abroad, where will your hearts go? You must not all move toward where the teacher is.

Wherever the teacher goes, he will pray for this nation and this people, and his heart will always be in Korea, so you must know that and take responsibility in place of the teacher to protect the present of this nation and this people and to fulfill the providential will of God for the entire nation and people, striving to complete the mission of the times. Therefore, we must overcome the present. Without overcoming the present, there is no victory. I hope you understand this.

<Prayer> Father! Please take care of your children gathered here. I hope that on this morning, you will take responsibility for the bond that allows us to envision a day when we can meet again.
Now, when we think that we must prepare the foundation that will become the defensive line and the launching pad to reach the pinnacle of the world in the 1980s, we feel that we are standing in a position where we cannot rest. When we consider that everything must be directed toward a public purpose, there are times when the path of our intentions feels quite tedious. However, since there is no other path but this one, Father, we must continue on. It is a mission that cannot be fulfilled by South Korea alone; we must go out into the world. Father, please be with us. We do not wish for anyone's protection. We do not wish for anyone's comfort. Our absolute wish is to leave your protection and your comfort for the nation and the world.

We must go. The youth must go in their own way, the middle-aged must go in their own way, and the elderly must go in their own way. We are in a position where we cannot afford not to go, as we are a Unification Church that is in a fate similar to that of refugees wandering in the historical era of the world. Since our enemies are guarding the front lines, we come to realize that the rugged valleys and lonely shadows are the only paths we must enter.

We have dedicated our lives to walking such a path until now. Indeed, it has been a pitiful path. All those who walk this path of intention are pitiful people. Father, we know well that because you walk such a path, we who follow you cannot escape the shared fate of walking such a path. Therefore, your valley of tears cannot be separate from our valley of tears, and your place of misery cannot be separate from our place of misery. When you give the command to attack, the time has come for us to lay everything on the line and launch our attack.

Now we must unite. We understand that Abel cannot meet the parents without gathering Cain. When we think of the 38th parallel that divides the Cain nation and the Abel nation to welcome the national parents, we know that we are lined up for the day when these two nations can be liberated.

When we consider that you have entrusted us with the mission to usher in a day when your holy will can raise the flag of victory, allowing us to lay everything bare and laugh, and to sing the song of triumph with all our strength, we realize that you, looking at us, are a pitiful being. We did not know how anxious you must be as you look at us.

Father, we will go. We are already resolved beings, determined to tread the path of destiny that you have left behind. It is our wish to cross this hill before we die. Even if it means becoming disabled, we know we must not die; even if we are wounded, no matter what humiliation we endure, we must cross this hill. It is not the time to discuss the difficulties of the past, but the time to resolve to overcome the difficult path of tomorrow. O Father, who knows this mission! Please protect the children scattered across the nation. When we think of how significant our mission is this year and next year, we earnestly ask you to guide us along the path of responsibility.

We know that you will not allow us to meet the fate of the defeated, so to avoid that fate, we must be more tenacious than the communist world of Satan. We must have more fighting spirit. We must fight with a heart of filial piety and the loyalty of a faithful servant. When we think of this, we must unite more. Strengthening our organization is our mission. We earnestly request and hope that you will allow us to remain as a group that can be remembered by you, having adorned the early 1970s in any department.

Please personally oversee everything. Until we meet again, we earnestly ask for your guidance. Whenever we meet those we can meet, we hope that your glory will be with us, and we pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.
